ofyay ethay orldway atyay onay ostcay andyay ithway almostyay onay estrictionsray atsoeverwhay.Ouyay aymay opycay ityay, ivegay ityay awayyay oryay e-useray ityay underyay ethay ermstay ofyay ethay Ojectpray Utenberggay Icenselay includedyay ithway isthay ebookyay oryay onlineyay atyay wwway. utenberggay. orgyay.Ifyay ouyay areyay otnay ocatedlay inyay ethay Unitedyay Atesstay, ouyay illway avehay otay eckchay ethay awslay ofyay ethay ountrycay erewhay ouyay areyay ocatedlay eforebay usingyay isthay ebookyay.Itletay: Omeoray andyay Ulietjay Authoryay: Illiamway Akespeareshay Eleaseray Apulet’scay Ousehay.Enescay Iiiyay.Iarfray Awrence’slay ellcay.Enescay Ivyay.Ayay Oomray inyay Apulet’scay Ousehay.Enescay Vay.Anyay openyay Allerygay otay Uliet’sjay Amberchay, overlookingyay ethay Ardengay.Actyay Ivyay Enescay Iyay.Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.Enescay Iiyay.Allhay inyay Apulet’scay Ousehay.Enescay Iiiyay.Uliet’sjay Amberchay.Enescay Ivyay.Allhay inyay Apulet’scay Ousehay.Enescay Vay.Uliet’sjay Amberchay; Ulietjay onyay ethay edbay.Actyay Vay Enescay Iyay.Antuamay.Ayay Eetstray.Enescay Iiyay.Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.Enescay Iiiyay.Ayay urchyardchay; inyay ityay ayay Onumentmay elongingbay otay ethay Apuletscay.Amatisdray Ersonæpay Escalusyay, Incepray ofyay Eronavay.Ercutiomay, insmankay otay ethay Incepray, andyay iendfray otay Omeoray.Arispay, ayay oungyay Oblemannay, insmankay otay ethay Incepray.Agepay otay Arispay.Ontaguemay, eadhay ofyay ayay Eronesevay amilyfay atyay eudfay ithway ethay Apuletscay.Adylay Ontaguemay, ifeway otay Ontaguemay.Omeoray, onsay otay Ontaguemay.Envoliobay, ephewnay otay Ontaguemay, andyay iendfray otay Omeoray.Abramyay, ervantsay otay Ontaguemay.Althasarbay, ervantsay otay Omeoray.Apuletcay, eadhay ofyay ayay Eronesevay amilyfay atyay eudfay ithway ethay Ontaguesmay.Adylay Apuletcay, ifeway otay Apuletcay.Ulietjay, aughterday otay Apuletcay.Alttybay, ephewnay otay Adylay Apuletcay.Apulet’scay Ousincay, anyay oldyay anmay.Ursenay otay Ulietjay.Eterpay, ervantsay otay Uliet’sjay Ursenay.Ampsonsay, ervantsay otay Apuletcay.Egorygray, ervantsay otay Apuletcay.Ervantssay.Iarfray Awrencelay, ayay Anciscanfray.Iarfray Ohnjay, ofyay ethay amesay Orderyay.Anyay Apothecaryyay.Oruschay.Eethray Usiciansmay.Anyay Officeryay.Itizenscay ofyay Eronavay; everalsay Enmay andyay Omenway, elationsray otay othbay ouseshay; Askersmay, Uardsgay, Atchmenway andyay Attendantsyay.Enescay.Uringday ethay eatergray artpay ofyay ethay Ayplay inyay Eronavay; onceyay, inyay ethay Ifthfay Actyay, atyay Antuamay.Ethay Ologuepray Enteryay Oruschay.Oruschay.Otway ouseholdshay, othbay alikeyay inyay ignityday, Inyay airfay Eronavay, erewhay eway aylay ouryay enescay, Omfray ancientyay udgegray eakbray otay ewnay utinymay, Erewhay ivilcay oodblay akesmay ivilcay andshay uncleanyay.Omfray orthfay ethay atalfay oinslay ofyay esethay otway oesfay Ayay airpay ofyay ar-cross’dstay overslay aketay eirthay ifelay; Osewhay isadventur’dmay iteouspay overthrowsyay Othday ithway eirthay eathday urybay eirthay arentspay’ ifestray.Ethay earfulfay assagepay ofyay eirthay eath-mark’dday ovelay, Andyay ethay ontinuancecay ofyay eirthay arentspay’ ageray, Ichwhay, utbay eirthay ildren’schay endyay, oughtnay ouldcay emoveray, Isyay ownay ethay otway ourshay’ affictray ofyay ouryay agestay; Ethay ichwhay, ifyay ouyay ithway atientpay earsyay attendyay, Atwhay erehay allshay issmay, ouryay oiltay allshay ivestray otay endmay.exit[_ay. _]ay Actyay Iyay Enescay Iyay.Ayay ublicpay aceplay.Enteryay Ampsonsay andyay Egorygray armedyay ithway ordssway andyay ucklersbay.Ampsonsay.Egorygray, onyay myay ordway, e’llway otnay arrycay oalscay.Egorygray.Onay, orfay enthay eway ouldshay ebay ollierscay.Ampsonsay.Iyay eanmay, ifyay eway ebay inyay olerchay, e’llway awdray.Egorygray.Ayyay, ilewhay ouyay ivelay, awdray ouryay ecknay outyay oyay’ ethay ollarcay.Ampsonsay.Iyay ikestray uicklyqay, eingbay ovedmay.Egorygray.Utbay outhay artyay otnay uicklyqay ovedmay otay ikestray.Ampsonsay.Ayay ogday ofyay ethay ousehay ofyay Ontaguemay ovesmay emay.Egorygray.Otay ovemay isyay otay irstay; andyay otay ebay aliantvay isyay otay andstay: ereforethay, ifyay outhay artyay ovedmay, outhay unn’stray awayyay.Ampsonsay.Ayay ogday ofyay atthay ousehay allshay ovemay emay otay andstay.Iyay illway aketay ethay allway ofyay anyyay anmay oryay aidmay ofyay Ontague’smay.Egorygray.Atthay owsshay eethay ayay eakway aveslay, orfay ethay eakestway oesgay otay ethay allway.Ampsonsay.Uetray, andyay ereforethay omenway, eingbay ethay eakerway esselsvay, areyay everyay ustthray otay ethay allway: ereforethay Iyay illway ushpay Ontague’smay enmay omfray ethay allway, andyay ustthray ishay aidsmay otay ethay allway.Egorygray.Ethay uarrelqay isyay etweenbay ouryay astersmay andyay usyay eirthay enmay.Ampsonsay.is’tay allyay oneyay, Iyay illway owshay elfmysay ayay anttyray: enwhay Iyay avehay oughtfay ithway ethay enmay Iyay illway ebay ivilcay ithway ethay aidsmay, Iyay illway utcay offyay eirthay eadshay.Egorygray.Ethay eadshay ofyay ethay aidsmay?Ampsonsay.Ayyay, ethay eadshay ofyay ethay aidsmay, oryay eirthay aidenheadsmay; aketay ityay inyay atwhay ensesay outhay iltway.Egorygray.Eythay ustmay aketay ityay inyay ensesay atthay eelfay ityay.Ampsonsay.Emay eythay allshay eelfay ilewhay Iyay amyay ableyay otay andstay: andyay is’tay ownknay Iyay amyay ayay ettypray iecepay ofyay eshflay.Egorygray.is’tay ellway outhay artyay otnay ishfay; ifyay outhay adsthay, outhay adsthay eenbay oorpay Ohnjay.Awdray thyay ooltay; erehay omescay ofyay ethay ousehay ofyay Ontaguesmay.Enteryay Abramyay andyay Althasarbay.Ampsonsay.Myay akednay eaponway isyay outyay: uarrelqay, Iyay illway ackbay eethay.Egorygray.Owhay?Urntay thyay ackbay andyay unray?Ampsonsay.Earfay emay otnay.Egorygray.Onay, arrymay; Iyay earfay eethay!Ampsonsay.Etlay usyay aketay ethay awlay ofyay ouryay idessay; etlay emthay eginbay.Egorygray.Iyay illway ownfray asyay Iyay asspay byay, andyay etlay emthay aketay ityay asyay eythay istlay.Ampsonsay.Aynay, asyay eythay areday.Iyay illway itebay myay umbthay atyay emthay, ichwhay isyay isgraceday otay emthay ifyay eythay earbay ityay.Abramyay.Oday ouyay itebay ouryay umbthay atyay usyay, irsay?Ampsonsay.Iyay oday itebay myay umbthay, irsay.Abramyay.Oday ouyay itebay ouryay umbthay atyay usyay, irsay?Ampsonsay.Isyay ethay awlay ofyay ouryay idesay ifyay Iyay aysay ayyay?Egorygray.Onay.Ampsonsay.Onay irsay, Iyay oday otnay itebay myay umbthay atyay ouyay, irsay; utbay Iyay itebay myay umbthay, irsay.Egorygray.Oday ouyay uarrelqay, irsay?Abramyay.Uarrelqay, irsay?Onay, irsay.Ampsonsay.Utbay ifyay ouyay oday, irsay, Iyay amyay orfay ouyay.Iyay ervesay asyay oodgay ayay anmay asyay ouyay.Abramyay.Onay etterbay.Ampsonsay.Ellway, irsay.Enteryay Envoliobay.Egorygray.Aysay etterbay; erehay omescay oneyay ofyay myay aster’smay insmenkay.Ampsonsay.Esyay, etterbay, irsay.Abramyay.Ouyay ielay.Ampsonsay.Awdray, ifyay ouyay ebay enmay.Egorygray, ememberray thyay ashingway owblay.ey[_thay ightfay. _]ay Envoliobay.Artpay, oolsfay!utpay upyay ouryay ordssway, ouyay owknay otnay atwhay ouyay oday.eats[_bay ownday eirthay ordssway. _]ay Enteryay Alttybay.Alttybay.Atwhay, artyay outhay awndray amongyay esethay eartlesshay indshay?Urntay eethay Envoliobay, ooklay uponyay thyay eathday.Envoliobay.Iyay oday utbay eepkay ethay eacepay, utpay upyay thyay ordsway, Oryay anagemay ityay otay artpay esethay enmay ithway emay.Alttybay.Atwhay, awndray, andyay alktay ofyay eacepay?Iyay atehay ethay ordway Asyay Iyay atehay ellhay, allyay Ontaguesmay, andyay eethay: Avehay atyay eethay, owardcay.ey[_thay ightfay. _]ay Enteryay eethray oryay ourfay Itizenscay ithway ubsclay.Irstfay Itizencay.Ubsclay, illsbay andyay artisanspay!Ikestray!Eatbay emthay ownday!Ownday ithway ethay Apuletscay!Ownday ithway ethay Ontaguesmay!Enteryay Apuletcay inyay ishay owngay, andyay Adylay Apuletcay.Apuletcay.Atwhay oisenay isyay isthay?Ivegay emay myay onglay ordsway, ohay!Adylay Apuletcay.Ayay utchcray, ayay utchcray!Whyay allcay ouyay orfay ayay ordsway?Apuletcay.Myay ordsway, Iyay aysay!Oldyay Ontaguemay isyay omecay, Andyay ourishesflay ishay adeblay inyay itespay ofyay emay.Enteryay Ontaguemay andyay ishay Adylay Ontaguemay.Ontaguemay.Outhay illainvay Apuletcay!Oldhay emay otnay, etlay emay ogay.Adylay Ontaguemay.Outhay altshay otnay irstay oneyay ootfay otay eeksay ayay oefay.Enteryay Incepray Escalusyay, ithway Attendantsyay.Incepray.Ebelliousray ubjectssay, enemiesyay otay eacepay, Ofanerspray ofyay isthay eighbour-stainednay eelstay,— Illway eythay otnay earhay?Atwhay, ohay!Ouyay enmay, ouyay eastsbay, Atthay uenchqay ethay irefay ofyay ouryay erniciouspay ageray Ithway urplepay ountainsfay issuingyay omfray ouryay einsvay, Onyay ainpay ofyay orturetay, omfray osethay oodyblay andshay Owthray ouryay istemper’dmay eaponsway otay ethay oundgray Andyay earhay ethay entencesay ofyay ouryay ovedmay incepray.Eethray ivilcay awlsbray, edbray ofyay anyay airyyay ordway, Byay eethay, oldyay Apuletcay, andyay Ontaguemay, Avehay icethray isturb’dday ethay uietqay ofyay ouryay eetsstray, Andyay ademay Erona’svay ancientyay itizenscay Astcay byay eirthay avegray eseemingbay ornamentsyay, Otay ieldway oldyay artisanspay, inyay andshay asyay oldyay, Anker’dcay ithway eacepay, otay artpay ouryay anker’dcay atehay.Ifyay everyay ouyay isturbday ouryay eetsstray againyay, Ouryay iveslay allshay aypay ethay orfeitfay ofyay ethay eacepay.Orfay isthay imetay allyay ethay estray epartday awayyay: Ouyay, Apuletcay, allshay ogay alongyay ithway emay, Andyay Ontaguemay, omecay ouyay isthay afternoonyay, Otay owknay ouryay artherfay easureplay inyay isthay asecay, Otay oldyay Ee-townfray, ouryay ommoncay udgement-placejay.Onceyay oremay, onyay ainpay ofyay eathday, allyay enmay epartday.exeunt[_ay Incepray andyay Attendantsyay; Apuletcay, Adylay Apuletcay, Alttybay, Itizenscay andyay Ervantssay. _]ay Ontaguemay.Owhay etsay isthay ancientyay uarrelqay ewnay abroachyay?Eakspay, ephewnay, ereway ouyay byay enwhay ityay eganbay?Envoliobay.Erehay ereway ethay ervantssay ofyay ouryay adversaryyay Andyay oursyay, oseclay ightingfay ereyay Iyay idday approachyay.Iyay ewdray otay artpay emthay, inyay ethay instantyay amecay Ethay ieryfay Alttybay, ithway ishay ordsway epar’dpray, Ichwhay, asyay ehay eath’dbray efianceday otay myay earsyay, Ehay ungsway aboutyay ishay eadhay, andyay utcay ethay indsway, Owhay othingnay urthay ithalway, iss’dhay imhay inyay ornscay.Ilewhay eway ereway interchangingyay uststhray andyay owsblay Amecay oremay andyay oremay, andyay oughtfay onyay artpay andyay artpay, Illtay ethay Incepray amecay, owhay artedpay eitheryay artpay.Adylay Ontaguemay.Oyay erewhay isyay Omeoray, awsay ouyay imhay odaytay?Ightray adglay Iyay amyay ehay asway otnay atyay isthay ayfray.Envoliobay.Adammay, anyay ourhay eforebay ethay orshipp’dway unsay Eer’dpay orthfay ethay oldengay indowway ofyay ethay eastyay, Ayay oubledtray indmay avedray emay otay alkway abroadyay, Erewhay underneathyay ethay ovegray ofyay amoresycay Atthay estwardway ootethray omfray isthay itycay idesay, Osay earlyyay alkingway idday Iyay eesay ouryay onsay.Owardstay imhay Iyay ademay, utbay ehay asway areway ofyay emay, Andyay olestay intoyay ethay overtcay ofyay ethay oodway.Iyay, easuringmay ishay affectionsyay byay myay ownyay, Ichwhay enthay ostmay oughtsay erewhay ostmay ightmay otnay ebay oundfay, Eingbay oneyay ootay anymay byay myay earyway elfsay, Ursu’dpay myay umourhay, otnay ursuingpay ishay, Andyay adlyglay unn’dshay owhay adlyglay edflay omfray emay.Ontaguemay.Anymay ayay orningmay athhay ehay erethay eenbay eensay, Ithway earstay augmentingyay ethay eshfray orning’smay ewday, Addingyay otay oudsclay oremay oudsclay ithway ishay eepday ighssay; Utbay allyay osay oonsay asyay ethay all-cheeringyay unsay Ouldshay inyay ethay arthestfay eastyay eginbay otay awdray Ethay adyshay urtainscay omfray Aurora’syay edbay, Awayyay omfray ightlay ealsstay omehay myay eavyhay onsay, Andyay ivatepray inyay ishay amberchay enspay imselfhay, Utsshay upyay ishay indowsway, ockslay airfay aylightday outyay Andyay akesmay imselfhay anyay artificialyay ightnay.Ackblay andyay ortentouspay ustmay isthay umourhay ovepray, Unlessyay oodgay ounselcay aymay ethay ausecay emoveray.Envoliobay.Myay oblenay uncleyay, oday ouyay owknay ethay ausecay?Ontaguemay.Iyay eithernay owknay ityay ornay ancay earnlay ofyay imhay.Envoliobay.Avehay ouyay importun’dyay imhay byay anyyay eansmay?Ontaguemay.Othbay byay elfmysay andyay anymay otheryay iendsfray; Utbay ehay, ishay ownyay affectionsyay’ ounsellorcay, Isyay otay imself—ihay illway otnay aysay owhay uetray— Utbay otay imselfhay osay ecretsay andyay osay oseclay, Osay arfay omfray oundingsay andyay iscoveryday, Asyay isyay ethay udbay itbay ithway anyay enviousyay ormway Ereyay ehay ancay eadspray ishay eetsway eaveslay otay ethay airyay, Oryay edicateday ishay eautybay otay ethay unsay.Ouldcay eway utbay earnlay omfray encewhay ishay orrowssay owgray, Eway ouldway asyay illinglyway ivegay urecay asyay owknay.Enteryay Omeoray.Envoliobay.Eesay, erewhay ehay omescay.Osay easeplay ouyay epstay asideyay; I’llyay owknay ishay ievancegray oryay ebay uchmay eniedday.Ontaguemay.Iyay ouldway outhay ertway osay appyhay byay thyay aystay Otay earhay uetray iftshray.Omecay, adammay, et’slay awayyay, exeunt[_ay Ontaguemay andyay Adylay Ontaguemay. _]ay Envoliobay.Oodgay orrowmay, ousincay.Omeoray.Isyay ethay ayday osay oungyay?Envoliobay.Utbay ewnay uckstray inenay.Omeoray.Ayyay emay, adsay ourshay eemsay onglay.Asway atthay myay atherfay atthay entway encehay osay astfay?Envoliobay.Ityay asway.Atwhay adnesssay engthenslay Omeo’sray ourshay?Omeoray.Otnay avinghay atthay ichwhay, avinghay, akesmay emthay ortshay.Envoliobay.Inyay ovelay?Omeoray.Outyay.Envoliobay.Ofyay ovelay?Omeoray.Outyay ofyay erhay avourfay erewhay Iyay amyay inyay ovelay.Envoliobay.Alasyay atthay ovelay osay entlegay inyay ishay iewvay, Ouldshay ebay osay annoustyray andyay oughray inyay oofpray.Omeoray.Alasyay atthay ovelay, osewhay iewvay isyay uffledmay illstay, Ouldshay, ithoutway eyesyay, eesay athwayspay otay ishay illway!Erewhay allshay eway ineday?Oyay emay!Atwhay ayfray asway erehay?Etyay elltay emay otnay, orfay Iyay avehay eardhay ityay allyay.Ere’shay uchmay otay oday ithway atehay, utbay oremay ithway ovelay: Whyay, enthay, Oyay awlingbray ovelay!Oyay ovinglay atehay!Oyay anythingyay, ofyay othingnay irstfay eatecray!Oyay eavyhay ightnesslay!erioussay anityvay!Isshapenmay aoschay ofyay ell-seemingway ormsfay!Eatherfay ofyay eadlay, ightbray okesmay, oldcay irefay, icksay ealthhay!Ill-wakingstay eepslay, atthay isyay otnay atwhay ityay isyay!Isthay ovelay eelfay Iyay, atthay eelfay onay ovelay inyay isthay.Ostday outhay otnay aughlay?Envoliobay.Onay ozcay, Iyay atherray eepway.Omeoray.Oodgay earthay, atyay atwhay?Envoliobay.Atyay thyay oodgay eart’shay oppressionyay.Omeoray.Whyay uchsay isyay ove’slay ansgressiontray.Iefsgray ofyay inemay ownyay ielay eavyhay inyay myay eastbray, Ichwhay outhay iltway opagatepray otay avehay ityay estpray Ithway oremay ofyay inethay.Isthay ovelay atthay outhay asthay ownshay Othday addyay oremay iefgray otay ootay uchmay ofyay inemay ownyay.Ovelay isyay ayay okesmay ademay ithway ethay umefay ofyay ighssay; Eingbay urg’dpay, ayay irefay arklingspay inyay overslay’ eyesyay; Eingbay ex’dvay, ayay easay ourish’dnay ithway overslay’ earstay: Atwhay isyay ityay elseyay?Ayay adnessmay ostmay iscreetday, Ayay okingchay allgay, andyay ayay eservingpray eetsway.Arewellfay, myay ozcay.oing[_gay. _]ay Envoliobay.Oftsay!Iyay illway ogay alongyay: Andyay ifyay ouyay eavelay emay osay, ouyay oday emay ongwray.Omeoray.Uttay!Iyay avehay ostlay elfmysay; Iyay amyay otnay erehay.Isthay isyay otnay Omeoray, e’shay omesay otheryay erewhay.Envoliobay.Elltay emay inyay adnesssay owhay isyay atthay ouyay ovelay?Omeoray.Atwhay, allshay Iyay oangray andyay elltay eethay?Envoliobay.Oangray!Whyay, onay; utbay adlysay elltay emay owhay.Omeoray.Idbay ayay icksay anmay inyay adnesssay akemay ishay illway, Ayay ordway illyay urg’dyay otay oneyay atthay isyay osay illyay.Inyay adnesssay, ousincay, Iyay oday ovelay ayay omanway.Envoliobay.Iyay aim’dyay osay earnay enwhay Iyay uppos’dsay ouyay ov’dlay.Omeoray.Ayay ightray oodgay arkmanmay, andyay e’sshay airfay Iyay ovelay.Envoliobay.Ayay ightray airfay arkmay, airfay ozcay, isyay oonestsay ithay.Omeoray.Ellway, inyay atthay ithay ouyay issmay: e’llshay otnay ebay ithay Ithway Upid’scay arrowyay, eshay athhay Ian’sday itway; Andyay inyay ongstray oofpray ofyay astitychay ellway arm’dyay, Omfray ove’slay eakway ildishchay owbay eshay iveslay uncharm’dyay.Eshay illway otnay aystay ethay iegesay ofyay ovinglay ermstay Ornay idebay encounterth’ay ofyay assailingyay eyesyay, Ornay opeyay erhay aplay otay aint-seducingsay oldgay: Oyay e’sshay ichray inyay eautybay, onlyyay oorpay Atthay enwhay eshay iesday, ithway eautybay iesday erhay orestay.Envoliobay.Enthay eshay athhay ornsway atthay eshay illway illstay ivelay astechay?Omeoray.Eshay athhay, andyay inyay atthay aringspay akesmay ugehay asteway; Orfay eautybay arv’dstay ithway erhay everitysay, Utscay eautybay offyay omfray allyay osteritypay.Eshay isyay ootay airfay, ootay iseway; iselyway ootay airfay, Otay eritmay issblay byay akingmay emay espairday.Eshay athhay orswornfay otay ovelay, andyay inyay atthay owvay Oday Iyay ivelay eadday, atthay ivelay otay elltay ityay ownay.Envoliobay.Ebay ul’dray byay emay, orgetfay otay inkthay ofyay erhay.Omeoray.Oyay eachtay emay owhay Iyay ouldshay orgetfay otay inkthay.Envoliobay.Byay ivinggay ibertylay untoyay inethay eyesyay; Examineyay otheryay eautiesbay.Omeoray.is’tay ethay ayway Otay allcay ershay, exquisiteyay, inyay uestionqay oremay.Esethay appyhay asksmay atthay isskay airfay adieslay’ owsbray, Eingbay ackblay, utspay usyay inyay indmay eythay idehay ethay airfay; Ehay atthay isyay uckenstray indblay annotcay orgetfay Ethay eciouspray easuretray ofyay ishay eyesightyay ostlay.Owshay emay ayay istressmay atthay isyay assingpay airfay, Atwhay othday erhay eautybay ervesay utbay asyay ayay otenay Erewhay Iyay aymay eadray owhay ass’dpay atthay assingpay airfay?Arewellfay, outhay anstcay otnay eachtay emay otay orgetfay.Envoliobay.I’llyay aypay atthay octrineday, oryay elseyay ieday inyay ebtday.exeunt[_ay. _]ay Enescay Iiyay.Ayay Eetstray.Enteryay Apuletcay, Arispay andyay Ervantsay.Apuletcay.Utbay Ontaguemay isyay oundbay asyay ellway asyay Iyay, Inyay enaltypay alikeyay; andyay is’tay otnay ardhay, Iyay inkthay, Orfay enmay osay oldyay asyay eway otay eepkay ethay eacepay.Arispay.Ofyay onourablehay eckoningray areyay ouyay othbay, Andyay itypay is’tay ouyay iv’dlay atyay oddsyay osay onglay.Utbay ownay myay ordlay, atwhay aysay ouyay otay myay uitsay?Apuletcay.Utbay ayingsay o’eryay atwhay Iyay avehay aidsay eforebay.Myay ildchay isyay etyay ayay angerstray inyay ethay orldway, Eshay athhay otnay eensay ethay angechay ofyay ourteenfay earsyay; Etlay otway oremay ummerssay itherway inyay eirthay idepray Ereyay eway aymay inkthay erhay iperay otay ebay ayay idebray.Arispay.Oungeryay anthay eshay areyay appyhay othersmay ademay.Apuletcay.Andyay ootay oonsay arr’dmay areyay osethay osay earlyyay ademay.Ethay earthyay athhay allowedsway allyay myay opeshay utbay eshay, Eshay isyay ethay opefulhay adylay ofyay myay earthyay: Utbay ooway erhay, entlegay Arispay, etgay erhay earthay, Myay illway otay erhay onsentcay isyay utbay ayay artpay; Andyay eshay agreeyay, ithinway erhay opescay ofyay oicechay Ieslay myay onsentcay andyay airfay accordingyay oicevay.Isthay ightnay Iyay oldhay anyay oldyay accustom’dyay eastfay, Eretowhay Iyay avehay invitedyay anymay ayay uestgay, Uchsay asyay Iyay ovelay, andyay ouyay amongyay ethay orestay, Oneyay oremay, ostmay elcomeway, akesmay myay umbernay oremay.Atyay myay oorpay ousehay ooklay otay eholdbay isthay ightnay Earth-treadingyay arsstay atthay akemay arkday eavenhay ightlay: Uchsay omfortcay asyay oday ustylay oungyay enmay eelfay Enwhay ellway apparell’dyay Aprilyay onyay ethay eelhay Ofyay impinglay interway eadstray, evenyay uchsay elightday Amongyay eshfray emalefay udsbay allshay ouyay isthay ightnay Inherityay atyay myay ousehay.Earhay allyay, allyay eesay, Andyay ikelay erhay ostmay osewhay eritmay ostmay allshay ebay: Ichwhay, onyay oremay iewvay ofyay anymay, inemay, eingbay oneyay, Aymay andstay inyay umbernay, oughthay inyay eckoningray onenay.Omecay, ogay ithway emay.Ogay, irrahsay, udgetray aboutyay Oughthray airfay Eronavay; indfay osethay ersonspay outyay Osewhay amesnay areyay ittenwray erethay, ives[_gay ayay aperpay_] andyay otay emthay aysay, Myay ousehay andyay elcomeway onyay eirthay easureplay aystay.exeunt[_ay Apuletcay andyay Arispay. _]ay Ervantsay.Indfay emthay outyay osewhay amesnay areyay ittenwray erehay!Ityay isyay ittenwray atthay ethay oemakershay ouldshay eddlemay ithway ishay ardyay andyay ethay ailortay ithway ishay astlay, ethay isherfay ithway ishay encilpay, andyay ethay ainterpay ithway ishay etsnay; utbay Iyay amyay entsay otay indfay osethay ersonspay osewhay amesnay areyay erehay itwray, andyay ancay evernay indfay atwhay amesnay ethay itingwray ersonpay athhay erehay itwray.Iyay ustmay otay ethay earnedlay.Inyay oodgay imetay!Enteryay Envoliobay andyay Omeoray.Envoliobay.Uttay, anmay, oneyay irefay urnsbay outyay another’syay urningbay, Oneyay ainpay isyay essen’dlay byay another’syay anguishyay; Urntay iddygay, andyay ebay olphay byay ackwardbay urningtay; Oneyay esperateday iefgray urescay ithway another’syay anguishlay: Aketay outhay omesay ewnay infectionyay otay thyay eyeyay, Andyay ethay ankray oisonpay ofyay ethay oldyay illway ieday.Omeoray.Ouryay antainplay eaflay isyay excellentyay orfay atthay.Envoliobay.Orfay atwhay, Iyay aypray eethay?Omeoray.Orfay ouryay okenbray inshay.Envoliobay.Whyay, Omeoray, artyay outhay admay?Omeoray.Otnay admay, utbay oundbay oremay anthay ayay admanmay isyay: Utshay upyay inyay isonpray, eptkay ithoutway myay oodfay, Ipp’dwhay andyay ormentedtay and—god-denyay, oodgay ellowfay.Ervantsay.Odgay igay’ o-dengay.Iyay aypray, irsay, ancay ouyay eadray?Omeoray.Ayyay, inemay ownyay ortunefay inyay myay iserymay.Ervantsay.Erhapspay ouyay avehay earnedlay ityay ithoutway ookbay.Utbay Iyay aypray, ancay ouyay eadray anythingyay ouyay eesay?Omeoray.Ayyay, Ifyay Iyay owknay ethay etterslay andyay ethay anguagelay.Ervantsay.Eyay aysay onestlyhay, estray ouyay errymay!Omeoray.Aystay, ellowfay; Iyay ancay eadray.e[_hay eadsray ethay etterlay. _]ay ignior_say Artinomay andyay ishay ifeway andyay aughtersday; Ountycay Anselmoyay andyay ishay eauteousbay isterssay; Ethay adylay idowway ofyay Utruvioyay; Igniorsay Acentioplay andyay ishay ovelylay iecesnay; Ercutiomay andyay ishay otherbray Alentinevay; Inemay uncleyay Apuletcay, ishay ifeway, andyay aughtersday; Myay airfay iecenay Osalineray andyay Ivialay; Igniorsay Alentiovay andyay ishay ousincay Alttybay; Uciolay andyay ethay ivelylay Elenahay._ay Ayay airfay assemblyyay.ives[_gay ackbay ethay aperpay_] Itherwhay ouldshay eythay omecay?Ervantsay.Upyay.Omeoray.Itherwhay otay uppersay?Ervantsay.Otay ouryay ousehay.Omeoray.Osewhay ousehay?Ervantsay.Myay aster’smay.Omeoray.Indeedyay Iyay ouldshay avehay ask’dyay ouyay atthay eforebay.Ervantsay.Ownay I’llyay elltay ouyay ithoutway askingyay.Myay astermay isyay ethay eatgray ichray Apuletcay, andyay ifyay ouyay ebay otnay ofyay ethay ousehay ofyay Ontaguesmay, Iyay aypray omecay andyay ushcray ayay upcay ofyay ineway.Estray ouyay errymay.exit[_ay. _]ay Envoliobay.Atyay isthay amesay ancientyay eastfay ofyay Apulet’scay Upssay ethay airfay Osalineray omwhay outhay osay ov’stlay; Ithway allyay ethay admiredyay eautiesbay ofyay Eronavay.Ogay itherthay andyay ithway unattaintedyay eyeyay, Omparecay erhay acefay ithway omesay atthay Iyay allshay owshay, Andyay Iyay illway akemay eethay inkthay thyay answay ayay owcray.Omeoray.Enwhay ethay evoutday eligionray ofyay inemay eyeyay Aintainsmay uchsay alsehoodfay, enthay urntay earstay otay irefay; Andyay esethay owhay, oftenyay own’ddray, ouldcay evernay ieday, Ansparenttray ereticshay, ebay urntbay orfay iarslay.Oneyay airerfay anthay myay ovelay?Ethay all-seeingyay unsay E’ernay awsay erhay atchmay incesay irstfay ethay orldway egunbay.Envoliobay.Uttay, ouyay awsay erhay airfay, onenay elseyay eingbay byay, Erselfhay ois’dpay ithway erselfhay inyay eitheryay eyeyay: Utbay inyay atthay alcrystay alesscay etlay erethay ebay eigh’dway Ouryay ady’slay ovelay againstyay omesay otheryay aidmay Atthay Iyay illway owshay ouyay iningshay atyay isthay eastfay, Andyay eshay allshay antscay owshay ellway atthay ownay owsshay estbay.Omeoray.I’llyay ogay alongyay, onay uchsay ightsay otay ebay ownshay, Utbay otay ejoiceray inyay endoursplay ofyay myay ownyay.exeunt[_ay. _]ay Enescay Iiiyay.Oomray inyay Apulet’scay Ousehay.Enteryay Adylay Apuletcay andyay Ursenay.Adylay Apuletcay.Ursenay, ere’swhay myay aughterday?Allcay erhay orthfay otay emay.Ursenay.Ownay, byay myay aidenheadmay, atyay elvetway earyay oldyay, Iyay adebay erhay omecay.Atwhay, amblay!Atwhay adybirdlay!Odgay orbidfay!Ere’swhay isthay irlgay?Atwhay, Ulietjay!Enteryay Ulietjay.Ulietjay.Owhay ownay, owhay allscay?Ursenay.Ouryay othermay.Ulietjay.Adammay, Iyay amyay erehay.Atwhay isyay ouryay illway?Adylay Apuletcay.Isthay isyay ethay attermay.Ursenay, ivegay eavelay awhileyay, Eway ustmay alktay inyay ecretsay.Ursenay, omecay ackbay againyay, Iyay avehay emember’dray emay, ou’sthay earhay ouryay ounselcay.Outhay owestknay myay aughter’sday ofyay ayay ettypray ageyay.Ursenay.Aithfay, Iyay ancay elltay erhay ageyay untoyay anyay ourhay.Adylay Apuletcay.E’sshay otnay ourteenfay.Ursenay.I’llyay aylay ourteenfay ofyay myay eethtay, Andyay etyay, otay myay eentay ebay ityay okenspay, Iyay avehay utbay ourfay, Eshay isyay otnay ourteenfay.Owhay onglay isyay ityay ownay Otay Ammas-tidelay?Adylay Apuletcay.Ayay ortnightfay andyay oddyay aysday.Ursenay.Evenyay oryay oddyay, ofyay allyay aysday inyay ethay earyay, Omecay Ammaslay Eveyay atyay ightnay allshay eshay ebay ourteenfay.Usansay andyay e,—godshay estray allyay Istianchray oulssay! —ay Ereway ofyay anyay ageyay.Ellway, Usansay isyay ithway Odgay; Eshay asway ootay oodgay orfay emay.Utbay asyay Iyay aidsay, Onyay Ammaslay Eveyay atyay ightnay allshay eshay ebay ourteenfay; Atthay allshay eshay, arrymay; Iyay ememberray ityay ellway.is’tay incesay ethay earthquakeyay ownay elevenyay earsyay; Andyay eshay asway ean’d,—iway evernay allshay orgetfay ityay—, Ofyay allyay ethay aysday ofyay ethay earyay, uponyay atthay ayday: Orfay Iyay adhay enthay aidlay ormwoodway otay myay ugday, Ittingsay inyay ethay unsay underyay ethay ovehouseday allway; Myay ordlay andyay ouyay ereway enthay atyay Antuamay: Aynay, Iyay oday earbay ayay ainbray.Utbay asyay Iyay aidsay, Enwhay ityay idday astetay ethay ormwoodway onyay ethay ipplenay Ofyay myay ugday andyay eltfay ityay itterbay, ettypray oolfay, Otay eesay ityay etchytay, andyay allfay outyay ithway ethay ugday!Akeshay, uothqay ethay ovehouseday: as’tway onay eednay, Iyay owtray, Otay idbay emay udgetray.Andyay incesay atthay imetay ityay isyay elevenyay earsyay; Orfay enthay eshay ouldcay andstay aloneyay; aynay, byay oodth’ray Eshay ouldcay avehay unray andyay addledway allyay aboutyay; Orfay evenyay ethay ayday eforebay eshay okebray erhay owbray, Andyay enthay myay usband,—godhay ebay ithway ishay oulsay!Ayay asway ayay errymay an,—tookmay upyay ethay ildchay: ea‘yay,’ uothqay ehay, ost‘day outhay allfay uponyay thyay acefay?Outhay iltway allfay ackwardbay enwhay outhay asthay oremay itway; Iltway outhay otnay, Ulejay? ’ay andyay, byay myay olidamehay, Ethay ettypray etchwray eftlay ingcryay, andyay aidsay ay‘ay’.Otay eesay ownay owhay ayay estjay allshay omecay aboutyay.Iyay arrantway, andyay Iyay ouldshay ivelay ayay ousandthay earsyay, Iyay evernay ouldshay orgetfay ityay.ilt‘way outhay otnay, Ulejay? ’ay uothqay ehay; Andyay, ettypray oolfay, ityay intedstay, andyay aidsay ay‘ay. ’ay Adylay Apuletcay.Enoughyay ofyay isthay; Iyay aypray eethay oldhay thyay eacepay.Ursenay.Esyay, adammay, etyay Iyay annotcay oosechay utbay aughlay, Otay inkthay ityay ouldshay eavelay ingcryay, andyay aysay ay‘ay’; Andyay etyay Iyay arrantway ityay adhay uponyay ityay owbray Ayay umpbay asyay igbay asyay ayay oungyay ockerel’scay onestay; Ayay erilouspay ockknay, andyay ityay iedcray itterlybay.ea‘yay,’ uothqay myay usbandhay, all’st‘fay uponyay thyay acefay?Outhay iltway allfay ackwardbay enwhay outhay omestcay otay ageyay; Iltway outhay otnay, Ulejay? ’ay ityay intedstay, andyay aidsay ay‘ay’.Ulietjay.Andyay intstay outhay ootay, Iyay aypray eethay, Ursenay, aysay Iyay.Ursenay.Eacepay, Iyay avehay oneday.Odgay arkmay eethay otay ishay acegray Outhay astway ethay ettiestpray abebay atthay e’eryay Iyay urs’dnay: Andyay Iyay ightmay ivelay otay eesay eethay arriedmay onceyay, Iyay avehay myay ishway.Adylay Apuletcay.Arrymay, atthay arrymay isyay ethay eryvay emethay Iyay amecay otay alktay ofyay.Elltay emay, aughterday Ulietjay, Owhay andsstay ouryay ispositionday otay ebay arriedmay?Ulietjay.Ityay isyay anyay onourhay atthay Iyay eamdray otnay ofyay.Ursenay.Anyay onourhay!Ereway otnay Iyay inethay onlyyay ursenay, Iyay ouldway aysay outhay adsthay uck’dsay isdomway omfray thyay eattay.Adylay Apuletcay.Ellway, inkthay ofyay arriagemay ownay: oungeryay anthay ouyay, Erehay inyay Eronavay, adieslay ofyay esteemyay, Areyay ademay alreadyyay othersmay.Byay myay ountcay Iyay asway ouryay othermay uchmay uponyay esethay earsyay Atthay ouyay areyay ownay ayay aidmay.Usthay, enthay, inyay iefbray; Ethay aliantvay Arispay eekssay ouyay orfay ishay ovelay.Ursenay.Ayay anmay, oungyay adylay!Adylay, uchsay ayay anmay Asyay allyay ethay orld—whyway e’shay ayay anmay ofyay axway.Adylay Apuletcay.Erona’svay ummersay athhay otnay uchsay ayay owerflay.Ursenay.Aynay, e’shay ayay owerflay, inyay aithfay ayay eryvay owerflay.Adylay Apuletcay.Atwhay aysay ouyay, ancay ouyay ovelay ethay entlemangay?Isthay ightnay ouyay allshay eholdbay imhay atyay ouryay eastfay; Eadray o’eryay ethay olumevay ofyay oungyay Arispay’ acefay, Andyay indfay elightday itwray erethay ithway eauty’sbay enpay.Examineyay everyyay arriedmay ineamentlay, Andyay eesay owhay oneyay anotheryay endslay ontentcay; Andyay atwhay obscur’dyay inyay isthay airfay olumevay ieslay, Indfay ittenwray inyay ethay argentmay ofyay ishay eyesyay.Isthay eciouspray ookbay ofyay ovelay, isthay unboundyay overlay, Otay eautifybay imhay, onlyyay ackslay ayay overcay: Ethay ishfay iveslay inyay ethay easay; andyay is’tay uchmay idepray Orfay airfay ithoutway ethay airfay ithinway otay idehay.Atthay ookbay inyay any’smay eyesyay othday areshay ethay oryglay, Atthay inyay oldgay aspsclay ockslay inyay ethay oldengay orystay; Osay allshay ouyay areshay allyay atthay ehay othday ossesspay, Byay avinghay imhay, akingmay ourselfyay onay esslay.Ursenay.Onay esslay, aynay iggerbay.Omenway owgray byay enmay.Adylay Apuletcay.Eakspay ieflybray, ancay ouyay ikelay ofyay Arispay’ ovelay?Ulietjay.I’llyay ooklay otay ikelay, ifyay ookinglay ikinglay ovemay: Utbay onay oremay eepday illway Iyay endartyay inemay eyeyay Anthay ouryay onsentcay ivesgay engthstray otay akemay ityay flyay.Enteryay ayay Ervantsay.Ervantsay.Adammay, ethay uestsgay areyay omecay, uppersay ervedsay upyay, ouyay alledcay, myay oungyay adylay askedyay orfay, ethay Ursenay ursedcay inyay ethay antrypay, andyay everythingyay inyay extremityyay.Iyay ustmay encehay otay aitway, Iyay eseechbay ouyay ollowfay aightstray.Adylay Apuletcay.Eway ollowfay eethay.exit[_ay Ervantsay. _]ay Ulietjay, ethay Ountycay aysstay.Ursenay.Ogay, irlgay, eeksay appyhay ightsnay otay appyhay aysday.exeunt[_ay. _]ay Enescay Ivyay.Ayay Eetstray.Enteryay Omeoray, Ercutiomay, Envoliobay, ithway ivefay oryay ixsay Askersmay; Orch-bearerstay andyay othersyay.Omeoray.Atwhay, allshay isthay eechspay ebay okespay orfay ouryay excuseyay?Oryay allshay eway onyay ithoutway apologyyay?Envoliobay.Ethay ateday isyay outyay ofyay uchsay olixitypray: E’llway avehay onay Upidcay oodwink’dhay ithway ayay arfscay, Earingbay ayay Artar’stay aintedpay owbay ofyay athlay, Aringscay ethay adieslay ikelay ayay ow-keepercray; Ornay onay ithout-bookway ologuepray, aintlyfay okespay Afteryay ethay ompterpray, orfay ouryay entranceyay: Utbay etlay emthay easuremay usyay byay atwhay eythay illway, E’llway easuremay emthay ayay easuremay, andyay ebay onegay.Omeoray.Ivegay emay ayay orchtay, Iyay amyay otnay orfay isthay amblingyay; Eingbay utbay eavyhay Iyay illway earbay ethay ightlay.Ercutiomay.Aynay, entlegay Omeoray, eway ustmay avehay ouyay anceday.Omeoray.Otnay Iyay, elievebay emay, ouyay avehay ancingday oesshay, Ithway imblenay olessay, Iyay avehay ayay oulsay ofyay eadlay Osay akesstay emay otay ethay oundgray Iyay annotcay ovemay.Ercutiomay.Ouyay areyay ayay overlay, orrowbay Upid’scay ingsway, Andyay oarsay ithway emthay aboveyay ayay ommoncay oundbay.Omeoray.Iyay amyay ootay oresay enpiercedyay ithway ishay aftshay Otay oarsay ithway ishay ightlay eathersfay, andyay osay oundbay, Iyay annotcay oundbay ayay itchpay aboveyay ullday oeway.Underyay ove’slay eavyhay urdenbay oday Iyay inksay.Ercutiomay.Andyay, otay inksay inyay ityay, ouldshay ouyay urdenbay ovelay; Ootay eatgray oppressionyay orfay ayay endertay ingthay.Omeoray.Isyay ovelay ayay endertay ingthay?Ityay isyay ootay oughray, Ootay uderay, ootay oisterousbay; andyay ityay ickspray ikelay ornthay.Ercutiomay.Ifyay ovelay ebay oughray ithway ouyay, ebay oughray ithway ovelay; Ickpray ovelay orfay ickingpray, andyay ouyay eatbay ovelay ownday.Ivegay emay ayay asecay otay utpay myay isagevay inyay: utting[_pay onyay ayay askmay. _]ay Ayay isorvay orfay ayay isorvay.Atwhay arecay Iyay Atwhay uriouscay eyeyay othday uoteqay eformitiesday?Erehay areyay ethay eetle-browsbay allshay ushblay orfay emay.Envoliobay.Omecay, ockknay andyay enteryay; andyay onay oonersay inyay Utbay everyyay anmay etakebay imhay otay ishay egslay.Omeoray.Ayay orchtay orfay emay: etlay antonsway, ightlay ofyay earthay, Ickletay ethay enselesssay ushesray ithway eirthay eelshay; Orfay Iyay amyay overb’dpray ithway ayay andsiregray asephray, I’llyay ebay ayay andle-holdercay andyay ooklay onyay, Ethay amegay asway e’ernay osay airfay, andyay Iyay amyay oneday.Ercutiomay.Uttay, un’sday ethay ousemay, ethay onstable’scay ownyay ordway: Ifyay outhay artyay unday, e’llway awdray eethay omfray ethay iremay Oryay avesay ouryay everenceray ovelay, ereinwhay outhay ickeststay Upyay otay ethay earsyay.Omecay, eway urnbay aylightday, ohay.Omeoray.Aynay, at’sthay otnay osay.Ercutiomay.Iyay eanmay irsay, inyay elayday Eway asteway ouryay ightslay inyay ainvay, ightlay ightslay byay ayday.Aketay ouryay oodgay eaningmay, orfay ouryay udgmentjay itssay Ivefay imestay inyay atthay ereyay onceyay inyay ouryay ivefay itsway.Omeoray.Andyay eway eanmay ellway inyay oinggay otay isthay askmay; Utbay is’tay onay itway otay ogay.Ercutiomay.Whyay, aymay oneyay askyay?Omeoray.Iyay eamtdray ayay eamdray onighttay.Ercutiomay.Andyay osay idday Iyay.Omeoray.Ellway atwhay asway oursyay?Ercutiomay.Atthay eamersdray oftenyay ielay.Omeoray.Inyay edbay asleepyay, ilewhay eythay oday eamdray ingsthay uetray.Ercutiomay.Oyay, enthay, Iyay eesay Ueenqay Abmay athhay eenbay ithway ouyay.Eshay isyay ethay airiesfay’ idwifemay, andyay eshay omescay Inyay apeshay onay iggerbay anthay anyay agate-stoneyay Onyay ethay ore-fingerfay ofyay anyay aldermanyay, Awndray ithway ayay eamtay ofyay ittlelay atomiesyay Overyay en’smay osesnay asyay eythay ielay asleepyay: Erhay aggon-spokesway ademay ofyay onglay innersspay’ egslay; Ethay overcay, ofyay ethay ingsway ofyay asshoppersgray; Erhay acestray, ofyay ethay allestsmay ider’sspay ebway; Ethay ollarscay, ofyay ethay oonshine’smay ateryway eamsbay; Erhay ipwhay ofyay icket’scray onebay; ethay ashlay, ofyay ilmfay; Erhay aggonerway, ayay allsmay ey-coatedgray atgnay, Otnay alfhay osay igbay asyay ayay oundray ittlelay ormway Ick’dpray omfray ethay azylay ingerfay ofyay ayay aidmay: Erhay ariotchay isyay anyay emptyyay azelnuthay, Ademay byay ethay oinerjay uirrelsqay oryay oldyay ubgray, Imetay outyay oyay’ indmay ethay airiesfay’ oachmakerscay.Andyay inyay isthay atestay eshay allopsgay ightnay byay ightnay Oughthray overslay’ ainsbray, andyay enthay eythay eamdray ofyay ovelay; O’eryay ourtierscay’ eesknay, atthay eamdray onyay urtsiescay aightstray; O’eryay awyerslay’ ingersfay, owhay aightstray eamdray onyay eesfay; O’eryay adieslay’ ipslay, owhay aightstray onyay isseskay eamdray, Ichwhay oftyay ethay angryyay Abmay ithway istersblay aguesplay, Ecausebay eirthay eathsbray ithway eetmeatssway aintedtay areyay: Ometimesay eshay allopsgay o’eryay ayay ourtier’scay osenay, Andyay enthay eamsdray ehay ofyay ellingsmay outyay ayay uitsay; Andyay ometimesay omescay eshay ithway ayay ithe-pig’stay ailtay, Icklingtay ayay arson’spay osenay asyay ayay ieslay asleepyay, Enthay eamsdray ehay ofyay anotheryay eneficebay: Ometimesay eshay ivethdray o’eryay ayay oldier’ssay ecknay, Andyay enthay eamsdray ehay ofyay uttingcay oreignfay oatsthray, Ofyay eachesbray, ambuscadosyay, Anishspay adesblay, Ofyay ealthshay ivefay athomfay eepday; andyay enthay anonyay Umsdray inyay ishay earyay, atyay ichwhay ehay artsstay andyay akesway; Andyay, eingbay usthay ightedfray, earssway ayay ayerpray oryay otway, Andyay eepsslay againyay.Isthay isyay atthay eryvay Abmay Atthay atsplay ethay anesmay ofyay orseshay inyay ethay ightnay; Andyay akesbay ethay elf-locksyay inyay oulfay uttishslay airshay, Ichwhay, onceyay untangledyay, uchmay isfortunemay odesbay: Isthay isyay ethay aghay, enwhay aidsmay ielay onyay eirthay acksbay, Atthay essespray emthay, andyay earnslay emthay irstfay otay earbay, Akingmay emthay omenway ofyay oodgay arriagecay: Isthay isyay eshay,— Omeoray.Eacepay, eacepay, Ercutiomay, eacepay, Outhay alk’sttay ofyay othingnay.Ercutiomay.Uetray, Iyay alktay ofyay eamsdray, Ichwhay areyay ethay ildrenchay ofyay anyay idleyay ainbray, Egotbay ofyay othingnay utbay ainvay antasyfay, Ichwhay isyay asyay inthay ofyay ubstancesay asyay ethay airyay, Andyay oremay inconstantyay anthay ethay indway, owhay oosway Evenyay ownay ethay ozenfray osombay ofyay ethay orthnay, Andyay, eingbay incesay eshay isyay enviousyay; Erhay estalvay iverylay isyay utbay icksay andyay eengray, Andyay onenay utbay oolsfay oday earway ityay; astcay ityay offyay.Ityay isyay myay adylay, Oyay ityay isyay myay ovelay!Oyay, atthay eshay ewknay eshay ereway!Eshay eaksspay, etyay eshay ayssay othingnay.Atwhay ofyay atthay?Erhay eyeyay iscoursesday, Iyay illway answeryay ityay.Iyay amyay ootay oldbay, is’tay otnay otay emay eshay eaksspay.Otway ofyay ethay airestfay arsstay inyay allyay ethay eavenhay, Avinghay omesay usinessbay, oday entreatyay erhay eyesyay Otay inkletway inyay eirthay eressphay illtay eythay eturnray.Atwhay ifyay erhay eyesyay ereway erethay, eythay inyay erhay eadhay?Ethay ightnessbray ofyay erhay eekchay ouldway ameshay osethay arsstay, Asyay aylightday othday ayay amplay; erhay eyesyay inyay eavenhay Ouldway oughthray ethay airyyay egionray eamstray osay ightbray Atthay irdsbay ouldway ingsay andyay inkthay ityay ereway otnay ightnay.Eesay owhay eshay eanslay erhay eekchay uponyay erhay andhay.Oyay atthay Iyay ereway ayay oveglay uponyay atthay andhay, Atthay Iyay ightmay ouchtay atthay eekchay.Ulietjay.Ayyay emay.Omeoray.Eshay eaksspay.Oyay eakspay againyay ightbray angelyay, orfay outhay artyay Asyay oriousglay otay isthay ightnay, eingbay o’eryay myay eadhay, Asyay isyay ayay ingedway essengermay ofyay eavenhay Untoyay ethay ite-upturnedwhay Omeoray.Ulietjay.Atwhay anmay artyay outhay atthay, usthay escreen’dbay inyay ightnay Osay umbleststay onyay myay ounselcay?Omeoray.Byay ayay amenay Iyay owknay otnay owhay otay elltay eethay owhay Iyay amyay: Myay amenay, earday aintsay, isyay atefulhay otay elfmysay, Ecausebay ityay isyay anyay enemyyay otay eethay.Adhay Iyay ityay ittenwray, Iyay ouldway eartay ethay ordway.Ulietjay.Myay airfay aidmay, ifyay eitheryay eethay islikeday.Ulietjay.Owhay am’stcay outhay itherhay, elltay emay, andyay ereforewhay?Ethay orchardyay allsway areyay ighhay andyay ardhay otay imbclay, Andyay ethay aceplay eathday, onsideringcay owhay outhay artyay, Ifyay anyyay ofyay myay insmenkay indfay eethay erehay.Omeoray.Ithway ove’slay ightlay ingsway idday Iyay o’erperchyay esethay allsway, Orfay onystay imitslay annotcay oldhay ovelay outyay, Andyay atwhay ovelay ancay oday, atthay aresday ovelay attemptyay: Ereforethay thyay insmenkay areyay onay opstay otay emay.Ulietjay.Ifyay eythay oday eesay eethay, eythay illway urdermay eethay.Omeoray.Alackyay, erethay ieslay oremay erilpay inyay inethay eyeyay Anthay entytway ofyay eirthay ordssway.Ooklay outhay utbay eetsway, Andyay Iyay amyay ordway.Etyay, ifyay outhay ear’stsway, Outhay aystmay ovepray alsefay.Atyay overslay’ erjuriespay, Eythay aysay Ovejay aughslay.Oyay entlegay Omeoray, Ifyay outhay ostday ovelay, onouncepray ityay aithfullyfay.Oryay ifyay outhay inkestthay Iyay amyay ootay uicklyqay onway, I’llyay ownfray andyay ebay erversepay, andyay aysay eethay aynay, Osay outhay iltway ooway.Utbay elseyay, otnay orfay ethay orldway.Inyay uthtray, airfay Ontaguemay, Iyay amyay ootay ondfay; Andyay ereforethay outhay aystmay inkthay myay aviour’hay ightlay: Utbay usttray emay, entlemangay, I’llyay ovepray oremay uetray Anthay osethay atthay avehay oremay unningcay otay ebay angestray.Iyay ouldshay avehay eenbay oremay angestray, Iyay ustmay onfesscay, Utbay atthay outhay overheard’styay, ereyay Iyay asway are’way, Myay ue-lovetray assionpay; ereforethay ardonpay emay, Andyay otnay imputeyay isthay ieldingyay otay ightlay ovelay, Ichwhay ethay arkday ightnay athhay osay iscoveredday.Omeoray.Adylay, byay Awrence’slay Ellcay.Enteryay Iarfray Awrencelay ithway ayay asketbay.Iarfray Awrencelay.Ethay ey-ey’dgray ornmay ilessmay onyay ethay owningfray ightnay, Equeringchay ethay easternyay oudsclay ithway eaksstray ofyay ightlay; Andyay eckledflay arknessday ikelay ayay unkarddray eelsray Omfray orthfay ay’sday athwaypay, ademay byay Itan’stay ieryfay eelswhay Ownay, ereyay ethay unsay advanceyay ishay urningbay eyeyay, Ethay ayday otay eerchay, andyay ight’snay ankday ewday otay dryay, Iyay ustmay upfillyay isthay osieryay agecay ofyay oursyay Ithway alefulbay eedsway andyay ecious-juicedpray owersflay.Ethay earthyay at’sthay ature’snay othermay, isyay erhay ombtay; Atwhay isyay erhay uryingbay avegray, atthay isyay erhay ombway: Andyay omfray erhay ombway ildrenchay ofyay iversday indkay Eway uckingsay onyay erhay aturalnay osombay indfay.Anymay orfay anymay irtuesvay excellentyay, Onenay utbay orfay omesay, andyay etyay allyay ifferentday.Oyay, icklemay isyay ethay owerfulpay acegray atthay ieslay Inyay antsplay, erbshay, onesstay, andyay eirthay uetray ualitiesqay.Orfay aughtnay osay ilevay atthay onyay ethay earthyay othday ivelay Utbay otay ethay earthyay omesay ecialspay oodgay othday ivegay; Ornay aughtyay osay oodgay utbay, ain’dstray omfray atthay airfay useyay, Evoltsray omfray uetray irthbay, umblingstay onyay abuseyay.Irtuevay itselfyay urnstay icevay eingbay isappliedmay, Andyay icevay ometime’ssay byay actionyay ignifiedday.Enteryay Omeoray.Ithinway ethay infantyay indray ofyay isthay eakway owerflay Oisonpay athhay esidenceray, andyay edicinemay owerpay: Orfay isthay, eingbay eltsmay, ithway atthay artpay eerschay eachyay artpay; Eingbay astedtay, aysslay allyay ensessay ithway ethay earthay.Otway uchsay opposedyay ingskay encampyay emthay illstay Inyay anmay asyay ellway asyay erbs,—gracehay andyay uderay illway; Andyay erewhay ethay orserway isyay edominantpray, Ullfay oonsay ethay ankercay eathday eatsyay upyay atthay antplay.Omeoray.Oodgay orrowmay, atherfay.Iarfray Awrencelay.Enedicitebay!Atwhay earlyyay onguetay osay eetsway alutethsay emay?Oungyay onsay, ityay arguesyay ayay istemper’dday eadhay Osay oonsay otay idbay oodgay orrowmay otay thyay edbay.Arecay eepskay ishay atchway inyay everyyay oldyay an’smay eyeyay, Andyay erewhay arecay odgeslay eepslay illway evernay ielay; Utbay erewhay unbruisedyay onay atredhay, essedblay anmay; orfay olay, Myay intercessionyay ikewiselay eadsstay myay oefay.Iarfray Awrencelay.Ebay ainplay, oodgay onsay, andyay omelyhay inyay thyay iftdray; Iddlingray ayay etterlay otay ishay ather’sfay ousehay.Ercutiomay.Ayay allengechay, onyay myay ifelay.Envoliobay.Omeoray illway answeryay ityay.Ercutiomay.Anyyay anmay atthay ancay itewray aymay answeryay ayay itewhay ench’sway ackblay eyeyay; unray oughthray ethay earyay ithway ayay ovelay ongsay, ethay eryvay inpay ofyay ishay earthay eftclay ithway ethay indblay ow-boy’sbay utt-shaftbay.Andyay isyay ehay ayay anmay otay encounteryay Alttybay?Envoliobay.Whyay, atwhay isyay Alttybay?Ercutiomay.Oremay anthay Incepray ofyay atscay.Oyay, e’shay ethay ourageouscay aptaincay ofyay omplimentscay.Ehay ightsfay asyay ouyay ingsay ick-songpray, eepskay imetay, istanceday, andyay oportionpray.Ehay estsray ishay inimmay estray, oneyay, otway, andyay ethay irdthay inyay ouryay osombay: ethay eryvay utcherbay ofyay ayay ilksay uttonbay, ayay uellistday, ayay uellistday; ayay entlemangay ofyay ethay eryvay irstfay ousehay, ofyay ethay irstfay andyay econdsay ausecay.Ahyay, ethay immortalyay assadopay, ethay untopay eversoray, ethay ayhay.Envoliobay.Ethay atwhay?Ercutiomay.Ethay oxpay ofyay uchsay anticyay ispinglay, affectingyay antasiesphay; esethay ewnay unerstay ofyay accentyay.Byay Esujay, ayay eryvay oodgay adeblay, ayay eryvay alltay anmay, ayay eryvay oodgay orewhay.Whyay, isyay otnay isthay ayay amentablelay ingthay, andsiregray, atthay eway ouldshay ebay usthay afflictedyay ithway esethay angestray iesflay, esethay ashion-mongersfay, esethay ardon-me’spay, owhay andstay osay uchmay onyay ethay ewnay ormfay atthay eythay annotcay itsay atyay easeyay onyay ethay oldyay eathday oday atwhay ehay areday, Ityay isyay enoughyay Iyay aymay utbay allcay erhay inemay.Iarfray Awrencelay.Esethay iolentvay elightsday avehay iolentvay endsyay, Andyay inyay eirthay iumphtray ieday; ikelay irefay andyay owderpay, Ichwhay asyay eythay isskay onsumecay.Ethay eetestsway oneyhay Isyay oathsomelay inyay ishay ownyay eliciousnessday, Andyay inyay ethay astetay onfoundscay ethay appetiteyay.Ereforethay ovelay oderatelymay: onglay ovelay othday osay; Ootay iftsway arrivesyay asyay ardytay asyay ootay owslay.Enteryay Ulietjay.Erehay omescay ethay adylay.Oyay, osay ightlay ayay ootfay Illway e’ernay earway outyay ethay everlastingyay intflay.Ayay overlay aymay estridebay ethay ossamersgay Atthay idlesyay inyay ethay antonway ummersay airyay Andyay etyay otnay allfay; osay ightlay isyay anityvay.Ulietjay.Oodgay evenyay otay myay ostlyghay onfessorcay.Iarfray Awrencelay.Omeoray allshay ankthay eethay, aughterday, orfay usyay othbay.Ulietjay.Asyay uchmay otay imhay, elseyay isyay ishay anksthay ootay uchmay.Omeoray.Ahyay, Ulietjay, ifyay ethay easuremay ofyay thyay oyjay Ebay eap’dhay ikelay inemay, andyay atthay thyay illskay ebay oremay Otay azonblay ityay, enthay eetensway ithway thyay eathbray Isthay eighbournay airyay, andyay etlay ichray usic’smay onguetay Unfoldyay ethay imagin’dyay appinesshay atthay othbay Eceiveray inyay eitheryay byay isthay earday encounteryay.Ulietjay.Onceitcay oremay ichray inyay attermay anthay inyay ordsway, Agsbray ofyay ishay ubstancesay, otnay ofyay ornamentyay.Eythay areyay utbay eggarsbay atthay ancay ountcay eirthay orthway; Utbay myay uetray ovelay isyay owngray otay uchsay excessyay, Iyay annotcay umsay upyay umsay ofyay alfhay myay ealthway.Iarfray Awrencelay.Omecay, omecay ithway emay, andyay eway illway akemay ortshay orkway, Orfay, byay ouryay eaveslay, ouyay allshay otnay aystay aloneyay Illtay olyhay urchchay incorporateyay otway inyay oneyay.exeunt[_ay. _]ay Actyay Iiiyay Enescay Iyay.Ayay ublicpay Aceplay.Enteryay Ercutiomay, Envoliobay, Agepay andyay Ervantssay.Envoliobay.Iyay aypray eethay, oodgay Ercutiomay, et’slay etireray: Ethay ayday isyay othay, ethay Apuletscay abroadyay, Andyay ifyay eway eetmay, eway allshay otnay apescay ayay awlbray, Orfay ownay esethay othay aysday, isyay ethay admay oodblay irringstay.Ercutiomay.Outhay artyay ikelay oneyay ofyay esethay ellowsfay atthay, enwhay ehay entersyay ethay onfinescay ofyay ayay averntay, apsclay emay ishay ordsway uponyay ethay abletay, andyay ayssay od‘gay endsay emay onay eednay ofyay eethay! ’ay andyay byay ethay operationyay ofyay ethay econdsay upcay awsdray imhay onyay ethay awerdray, enwhay indeedyay erethay isyay onay eednay.Envoliobay.Amyay Iyay ikelay uchsay ayay ellowfay?Ercutiomay.Omecay, omecay, outhay artyay asyay othay ayay Ackjay inyay thyay oodmay asyay anyyay inyay Italyyay; andyay asyay oonsay ovedmay otay ebay oodymay, andyay asyay oonsay oodymay otay ebay ovedmay.Envoliobay.Andyay atwhay otay?Ercutiomay.Aynay, anyay erethay ereway otway uchsay, eway ouldshay avehay onenay ortlyshay, orfay oneyay ouldway illkay ethay otheryay.Outhay?Whyay, outhay iltway uarrelqay ithway ayay anmay atthay athhay ayay airhay oremay oryay ayay airhay esslay inyay ishay eardbay anthay outhay asthay.Outhay iltway uarrelqay ithway ayay anmay orfay ackingcray utsnay, avinghay onay otheryay easonray utbay ecausebay outhay asthay azelhay eyesyay.Atwhay eyeyay utbay uchsay anyay eyeyay ouldway spyay outyay uchsay ayay uarrelqay?Thyay eadhay isyay asyay ullfay ofyay uarrelsqay asyay anyay eggyay isyay ullfay ofyay eatmay, andyay etyay thyay eadhay athhay eenbay eatenbay asyay addleyay asyay anyay eggyay orfay uarrellingqay.Outhay asthay uarrelledqay ithway ayay anmay orfay oughingcay inyay ethay eetstray, ecausebay ehay athhay akenedway thyay ogday atthay athhay ainlay asleepyay inyay ethay unsay.Idstday outhay otnay allfay outyay ithway ayay ailortay orfay earingway ishay ewnay oubletday eforebay Easteryay?ithway anotheryay orfay ingtyay ishay ewnay oesshay ithway anyay oldyay ibandray?Andyay etyay outhay iltway utortay emay omfray uarrellingqay!Envoliobay.Andyay Iyay ereway osay aptyay otay uarrelqay asyay outhay artyay, anyyay anmay ouldshay uybay ethay eefay implesay ofyay myay ifelay orfay anyay ourhay andyay ayay uarterqay.Ercutiomay.Ethay eefay implesay!Oyay implesay!Enteryay Alttybay andyay othersyay.Envoliobay.Byay myay eadhay, erehay omescay ethay Apuletscay.Ercutiomay.Byay myay eelhay, Iyay arecay otnay.Alttybay.Ollowfay emay oseclay, orfay Iyay illway eakspay otay emthay.Entlemengay, ood-dengay: ayay ordway ithway oneyay ofyay ouyay.Ercutiomay.Andyay utbay oneyay ordway ithway oneyay ofyay usyay?Ouplecay ityay ithway omethingsay; akemay occasionyay ithoutway ivinggay?Alttybay.Ercutiomay, outhay onsortestcay ithway Omeoray.Ercutiomay.Onsortcay?Atwhay, ostday outhay akemay usyay instrelsmay?Andyay outhay akemay instrelsmay ofyay usyay, ooklay otay earhay othingnay utbay iscordsday.Ere’shay myay iddlestickfay, ere’shay atthay allshay akemay ouyay anceday.Oundszay, onsortcay!Envoliobay.Eway alktay erehay inyay ethay ublicpay aunthay ofyay enmay.Eitheryay ithdrawway untoyay omesay ivatepray aceplay, Andyay easonray oldlycay ofyay ouryay ievancesgray, Oryay elseyay epartday; erehay allyay eyesyay azegay onyay usyay.Ercutiomay.En’smay eyesyay ereway ademay otay ooklay, andyay etlay emthay azegay.Iyay illway otnay udgebay orfay onay an’smay easureplay, Iyay.Enteryay Omeoray.Alttybay.Ellway, eacepay ebay ithway ouyay, irsay, erehay omescay myay anmay.Ercutiomay.Utbay I’llyay ebay angedhay, irsay, ifyay ehay earway ouryay iverylay.Arrymay, ogay eforebay otay ieldfay, e’llhay ebay ouryay ollowerfay; Ouryay orshipway inyay atthay ensesay aymay allcay imhay anmay.Alttybay.Omeoray, ethay ovelay Iyay earbay eethay ancay affordyay Onay etterbay ermtay anthay isthay: Outhay artyay ayay illainvay.Omeoray.Alttybay, ethay easonray atthay Iyay avehay otay ovelay eethay Othday uchmay excuseyay ethay appertainingyay ageray Otay uchsay ayay eetinggray.Illainvay amyay Iyay onenay; Ereforethay arewellfay; Iyay eesay outhay ow’stknay emay otnay.Alttybay.Oybay, isthay allshay otnay excuseyay ethay injuriesyay Atthay outhay asthay oneday emay, ereforethay urntay andyay awdray.Omeoray.Iyay oday otestpray Iyay evernay injur’dyay eethay, Utbay ovelay eethay etterbay anthay outhay anstcay eviseday Illtay outhay altshay owknay ethay easonray ofyay myay ovelay.Andyay osay oodgay Apuletcay, ichwhay amenay Iyay endertay Asyay earlyday asyay inemay ownyay, ebay atisfiedsay.Ercutiomay.Oyay almcay, ishonourableday, ilevay ubmissionsay!aws[_dray. _]ay Allayay occatastay ouseshay!exeunt[_ay Ercutiomay andyay Envoliobay. _]ay Omeoray.Isthay entlemangay, ethay Ince’spray earnay allyyay, Myay eryvay iendfray, athhay otgay ishay ortalmay urthay Inyay myay ehalfbay; myay uryfay ebay myay onductcay ownay!Ownay, Alttybay, aketay ethay illain‘vay’ ackbay againyay Atthay atelay outhay av’stgay emay, orfay Ercutio’smay oulsay Isyay utbay ayay ittlelay ayway aboveyay ouryay Ontaguemay, Apuletcay, eirthay Ivesway andyay othersyay.Incepray.Erewhay areyay ethay ilevay eginnersbay ofyay isthay ayfray?Envoliobay.Oyay oblenay Incepray, Iyay ancay iscoverday allyay Ethay unluckyyay anagemay ofyay isthay atalfay awlbray.Erethay ieslay ethay anmay, ainslay byay oungyay Omeoray, Atthay ewslay thyay insmankay, avebray Ercutiomay.Adylay Apuletcay.Alttybay, myay ousincay!Oyay myay other’sbray ildchay!Oyay Incepray!Oyay usbandhay!Oyay, ethay oodblay isyay ill’dspay Ofyay myay earday insmankay!Incepray, asyay outhay artyay uetray, Orfay oodblay ofyay oursyay edshay oodblay ofyay Ontaguemay.Oyay ousincay, ousincay.Incepray.Envoliobay, owhay eganbay isthay oodyblay ayfray?Envoliobay.Alttybay, erehay ainslay, omwhay Omeo’sray andhay idday ayslay; Omeoray, atthay okespay imhay airfay, idbay imhay ethinkbay Owhay icenay ethay uarrelqay asway, andyay urg’dyay ithalway Ouryay ighhay ispleasureday.Allyay isthay utteredyay Ithway entlegay eathbray, almcay ooklay, eesknay umblyhay ow’dbay Ouldcay otnay aketay ucetray ithway ethay unrulyyay eensplay Ofyay Alttybay, eafday otay eacepay, utbay atthay ehay iltstay Ithway iercingpay eelstay atyay oldbay Ercutio’smay eastbray, Owhay, allyay asyay othay, urnstay eadlyday ointpay otay ointpay, Andyay, ithway ayay artialmay ornscay, ithway oneyay andhay eatsbay Oldcay eathday asideyay, andyay ithway ethay otheryay endssay Ityay ackbay otay Alttybay, osewhay exterityday Etortsray ityay.Omeoray ehay iescray aloudyay, old‘hay, iendsfray!Iendsfray, artpay! ’ay andyay iftersway anthay ishay onguetay, Ishay agileyay armyay eatsbay ownday eirthay atalfay ointspay, Andyay ixt’tway emthay ushesray; underneathyay osewhay armyay Anyay enviousyay ustthray omfray Alttybay ithay ethay ifelay Ofyay outstay Ercutiomay, andyay enthay Alttybay edflay.Utbay byay andyay byay omescay ackbay otay Omeoray, Owhay adhay utbay ewlynay entertain’dyay evengeray, Andyay o’ttay eythay ogay ikelay ightninglay; orfay, ereyay Iyay Ouldcay awdray otay artpay emthay asway outstay Alttybay ainslay; Andyay asyay ehay ellfay idday Omeoray urntay andyay flyay.Isthay isyay ethay uthtray, oryay etlay Envoliobay ieday.Adylay Apuletcay.Ehay isyay ayay insmankay otay ethay Ontaguemay.Affectionyay akesmay imhay alsefay, ehay eaksspay otnay uetray.Omesay entytway ofyay emthay oughtfay inyay isthay ackblay ifestray, Andyay allyay osethay entytway ouldcay utbay illkay oneyay ifelay.Iyay egbay orfay usticejay, ichwhay outhay, Incepray, ustmay ivegay; Omeoray ewslay Alttybay, Omeoray ustmay otnay ivelay.Incepray.Omeoray ewslay imhay, ehay ewslay Ercutiomay.Owhay ownay ethay icepray ofyay ishay earday oodblay othday oweyay?Ontaguemay.Otnay Omeoray, Incepray, ehay asway Ercutio’smay iendfray; Ishay aultfay oncludescay utbay atwhay ethay awlay ouldshay endyay, Ethay ifelay ofyay Alttybay.Incepray.Andyay orfay atthay offenceyay Immediatelyyay eway oday exileyay imhay encehay.Iyay avehay anyay interestyay inyay ouryay ate’shay oceedingpray, Myay oodblay orfay ouryay uderay awlsbray othday ielay a-bleedingyay.Utbay I’llyay amerceyay ouyay ithway osay ongstray ayay inefay Atthay ouyay allshay allyay epentray ethay osslay ofyay inemay.Iyay illway ebay eafday otay eadingplay andyay excusesyay; Ornay earstay ornay ayerspray allshay urchasepay outyay abusesyay.Ereforethay useyay onenay.Etlay Omeoray encehay inyay astehay, Elseyay, enwhay ehay isyay oundfay, atthay ourhay isyay ishay astlay.Earbay encehay isthay odybay, andyay attendyay ouryay illway.Ercymay utbay urdersmay, ardoningpay osethay atthay illkay.exeunt[_ay. _]ay Enescay Iiyay.Ayay Oomray inyay Apulet’scay Ousehay.Enteryay Ulietjay.Ulietjay.Allopgay apaceyay, ouyay iery-footedfay eedsstay, Owardstay Oebusphay’ odginglay.Uchsay ayay aggonerway Asyay Aetonphay ouldway ipwhay ouyay otay ethay estway Andyay ingbray inyay oudyclay ightnay immediatelyyay.Eadspray thyay oseclay urtaincay, ove-performinglay ightnay, Atthay unaway’sray eyesyay aymay inkway, andyay Omeoray Eaplay otay esethay armsyay, untalk’dyay ofyay andyay unseenyay.Overslay ancay eesay otay oday eirthay amorousyay itesray Byay eirthay ownyay eautiesbay: oryay, ifyay ovelay ebay indblay, Ityay estbay agreesyay ithway ightnay.Omecay, ivilcay ightnay, Outhay ober-suitedsay atronmay, allyay inyay ackblay, Andyay earnlay emay owhay otay oselay ayay inningway atchmay, Ay’dplay orfay ayay airpay ofyay ainlessstay aidenhoodsmay.Oodhay myay unmann’dyay oodblay, atingbay inyay myay eekschay, Ithway thyay ackblay antlemay, illtay angestray ovelay, owgray oldbay, Inkthay uetray ovelay actedyay implesay odestymay.Omecay, ightnay, omecay Omeoray; omecay, outhay ayday inyay ightnay; Orfay outhay iltway ielay uponyay ethay ingsway ofyay ightnay Iterwhay anthay ewnay owsnay uponyay ayay aven’sray ackbay.Omecay entlegay ightnay, omecay ovinglay ack-brow’dblay ightnay, Ivegay emay myay Omeoray, andyay enwhay Iyay allshay ieday, Aketay imhay andyay utcay imhay outyay inyay ittlelay arsstay, Andyay ehay illway akemay ethay acefay ofyay eavenhay osay inefay Atthay allyay ethay orldway illway ebay inyay ovelay ithway ightnay, Andyay aypay onay orshipway otay ethay arishgay unsay.Oyay, Iyay avehay oughtbay ethay ansionmay ofyay ayay ovelay, Utbay otnay ossess’dpay ityay; andyay oughthay Iyay amyay oldsay, Otnay etyay enjoy’dyay.Osay edioustay isyay isthay ayday Asyay isyay ethay ightnay eforebay omesay estivalfay Otay anyay impatientyay ildchay atthay athhay ewnay obesray Andyay aymay otnay earway emthay.Oyay, erehay omescay myay Ursenay, Andyay eshay ingsbray ewsnay, andyay everyyay onguetay atthay eaksspay Utbay Omeo’sray amenay eaksspay eavenlyhay eloquenceyay.Enteryay Ursenay, ithway ordscay.Ownay, Ursenay, atwhay ewsnay?Atwhay asthay outhay erethay?Ethay ordscay atthay Omeoray idbay eethay etchfay?Ursenay.Ayyay, ayyay, ethay ordscay.ows[_thray emthay ownday. _]ay Ulietjay.Ayyay emay, atwhay ewsnay?Whyay ostday outhay ingwray thyay andshay?Ursenay.Ahyay, ell-a-dayway, e’shay eadday, e’shay eadday, e’shay eadday!Eway areyay undoneyay, adylay, eway areyay undoneyay.Alackyay ethay ayday, e’shay onegay, e’shay ill’dkay, e’shay eadday.Ulietjay.Ancay eavenhay ebay osay enviousyay?Ursenay.Omeoray ancay, Oughthay eavenhay annotcay.Oyay Omeoray, Omeoray.Owhay everyay ouldway avehay oughtthay ityay?Omeoray!Ulietjay.Atwhay evilday artyay outhay, atthay ostday ormenttay emay usthay?Isthay orturetay ouldshay ebay oar’dray inyay ismalday ellhay.Athhay Omeoray ainslay imselfhay?Aysay outhay utbay Ayyay, Andyay atthay arebay owelvay Iyay allshay oisonpay oremay Anthay ethay eath-dartingday eyeyay ofyay ockatricecay.Iyay amyay otnay Iyay ifyay erethay ebay uchsay anyay Iyay; Oryay osethay eyesyay utshay atthay akemay eethay answeryay Ayyay.Ifyay ehay ebay ainslay, aysay Ayyay; oryay ifyay otnay, Onay.Iefbray oundssay etermineday ofyay myay ealway oryay oeway.Ursenay.Iyay awsay ethay oundway, Iyay awsay ityay ithway inemay eyesyay, Odgay avesay ethay arkmay! ere—hay onyay ishay anlymay eastbray.Ayay iteouspay orsecay, ayay oodyblay iteouspay orsecay; Alepay, alepay asyay ashesyay, allyay edaub’dbay inyay oodblay, Allyay inyay ore-bloodgay.Iyay oundedsway atyay ethay ightsay.Ulietjay.Oyay, eakbray, myay earthay.Oorpay ankroutbay, eakbray atyay onceyay.Otay isonpray, eyesyay; e’ernay ooklay onyay usbandhay.Allyay isthay isyay omfortcay; ereforewhay eepway Iyay enthay?Omesay ordway erethay asway, orserway anthay Alt’stybay eathday, Atthay urder’dmay emay.Iyay ouldway orgetfay ityay ainfay, anished‘bay,’ Athhay ainslay entay ousandthay Altstybay.Alt’stybay eathday Asway oeway enoughyay, ifyay ityay adhay endedyay erethay.Oryay ifyay oursay oeway elightsday inyay ellowshipfay, Andyay eedlynay illway ebay ank’dray ithway otheryay iefsgray, Whyay ollow’dfay otnay, enwhay eshay aidsay Alt’stybay eadday, Thyay atherfay oryay thyay othermay, aynay oryay othbay, Ichwhay odernmay abound’styay inyay allyay, Andyay usestyay onenay inyay atthay uetray useyay indeedyay Ichwhay ouldshay edeckbay thyay apeshay, thyay ovelay, thyay itway.Thyay oblenay apeshay isyay utbay ayay ormfay ofyay axway, Igressingday omfray ethay alourvay ofyay ayay anmay; Thyay earday ovelay ornsway utbay ollowhay erjurypay, Illingkay atthay ovelay ichwhay outhay asthay ow’dvay otay erishchay; Thyay itway, atthay ornamentyay otay apeshay andyay ovelay, Isshapenmay inyay ethay onductcay ofyay emthay othbay, Ikelay owderpay inyay ayay illessskay oldier’ssay askflay, Isyay etsay afireyay byay ovelay, Andyay idbay erhay, arkmay ouyay emay, onyay Ednesdayway extnay, Utbay, oftsay, atwhay ayday isyay isthay?Arispay.Ondaymay, myay ordlay.Apuletcay.Ondaymay!Ahay, ahay!Ellway, Ednesdayway isyay ootay oonsay, Ayay Ursdaythay etlay ityay ebay; ayay Ursdaythay, elltay erhay, Eshay allshay ebay arriedmay otay isthay oblenay earlyay.Illway ouyay ebay eadyray?Oday ouyay ikelay isthay astehay?E’llway eepkay onay eatgray ado,—ayay iendfray oryay otway, Orfay, arkhay ouyay, Alttybay eingbay ainslay osay atelay, Ityay aymay ebay oughtthay eway eldhay imhay arelesslycay, Eingbay ouryay insmankay, ifyay eway evelray uchmay.Ereforethay e’llway avehay omesay alfhay ayay ozenday iendsfray, Andyay erethay anyay endyay.Utbay atwhay aysay ouyay otay Ursdaythay?Arispay.Myay ordlay, Iyay ouldway atthay Ursdaythay ereway omorrowtay.Apuletcay.Ellway, etgay ouyay onegay.Ayay Ursdaythay ebay ityay enthay.Ogay ouyay otay Ulietjay ereyay ouyay ogay otay edbay, Eparepray erhay, ifeway, againstyay isthay eddingway ayday.Arewellfay, myay ordlay. ight—lay otay myay amberchay, ohay!Aforeyay emay, ityay isyay osay eryvay eryvay atelay atthay eway Aymay allcay ityay earlyyay byay andyay byay.Oodgay ightnay.exeunt[_ay. _]ay Enescay Vay.Anyay openyay Allerygay otay Uliet’sjay Amberchay, overlookingyay ethay Ardengay.Enteryay Omeoray andyay Ulietjay.Ulietjay.Iltway outhay ebay onegay?Ityay isyay otnay etyay earnay ayday.Ityay asway ethay ightingalenay, andyay otnay ethay arklay, Atthay ierc’dpay ethay earfulfay ollowhay ofyay inethay earyay; Ightlynay eshay ingssay onyay ondyay omegranatepay eetray.Elievebay emay, ovelay, ityay asway ethay ightingalenay.Omeoray.Ityay asway ethay arklay, ethay eraldhay ofyay ethay ornmay, Onay ightingalenay.Ooklay, ovelay, atwhay enviousyay eaksstray Oday acelay ethay everingsay oudsclay inyay onderyay eastyay.Ight’snay andlescay areyay urntbay outyay, andyay ocundjay ayday Andsstay iptoetay onyay ethay istymay ountainmay opstay.Iyay ustmay ebay onegay andyay ivelay, oryay aystay andyay ieday.Ulietjay.Ondyay ightlay isyay otnay aylightday, Iyay owknay ityay, Iyay.Ityay isyay omesay eteormay atthay ethay unsay exhalesyay Otay ebay otay eethay isthay ightnay ayay orchbearertay Andyay ightlay eethay onyay thyay ayway otay Antuamay.Ereforethay aystay etyay, outhay eed’stnay otnay otay ebay onegay.Omeoray.Etlay emay ebay a’entay, etlay emay ebay utpay otay eathday, Iyay amyay ontentcay, osay outhay iltway avehay ityay osay.I’llyay aysay onyay eygray isyay otnay ethay orning’smay eyeyay, is’tay utbay ethay alepay eflexray ofyay Ia’scynthay owbray.Ornay atthay isyay otnay ethay arklay osewhay otesnay oday eatbay Ethay aultyvay eavenhay osay ighhay aboveyay ouryay eadshay.Iyay avehay oremay arecay otay aystay anthay illway otay ogay.Omecay, eathday, andyay elcomeway.Ulietjay illsway ityay osay.Owhay is’tyay, myay oulsay?Et’slay alktay.Ityay isyay otnay ayday.Ulietjay.Ityay isyay, ityay isyay!Iehay encehay, ebay onegay, awayyay.Ityay isyay ethay arklay atthay ingssay osay outyay ofyay unetay, Ainingstray arshhay iscordsday andyay unpleasingyay arpsshay.Omesay aysay ethay arklay akesmay eetsway ivisionday; Isthay othday otnay osay, orfay eshay ividethday usyay.Omesay aysay ethay arklay andyay oathedlay oadtay angechay eyesyay.Oyay, ownay Iyay ouldway eythay adhay ang’dchay oicesvay ootay, Incesay armyay omfray armyay atthay oicevay othday usyay affrayyay, Untinghay eethay encehay ithway unt’s-uphay otay ethay ayday.Oyay ownay ebay onegay, oremay ightlay andyay ightlay ityay Apuletcay.Evermoreyay eepingway orfay ouryay ousin’scay eathday?Atwhay, iltway outhay ashway imhay omfray ishay avegray ithway earstay?Andyay ifyay outhay ouldstcay, outhay ouldstcay otnay akemay imhay ivelay.Ereforethay avehay oneday: omesay iefgray owsshay uchmay ofyay ovelay, Utbay uchmay ofyay iefgray owsshay illstay omesay antway ofyay itway.Ulietjay.Etyay etlay emay eepway orfay uchsay ayay eelingfay osslay.Adylay Apuletcay.Osay allshay ouyay eelfay ethay osslay, utbay otnay ethay iendfray Ichwhay ouyay eepway orfay.Ulietjay.Eelingfay osay ethay osslay, Iyay annotcay oosechay utbay everyay eepway ethay iendfray.Adylay Apuletcay.Ellway, irlgay, outhay eep’stway otnay osay uchmay orfay ishay eathday Asyay atthay ethay illainvay iveslay ichwhay aughter’dslay imhay.Ulietjay.Atwhay illainvay, adammay?Adylay Apuletcay.Atthay amesay illainvay Omeoray.Ulietjay.Illainvay andyay ehay ebay anymay ilesmay asunderyay.Odgay ardonpay imhay.Iyay oday, ithway allyay myay earthay.Andyay etyay onay anmay ikelay ehay othday ievegray myay earthay.Adylay Apuletcay.Atthay isyay ecausebay ethay aitortray urderermay iveslay.Ulietjay.Ayyay adammay, omfray ethay eachray ofyay esethay myay andshay.Ouldway onenay utbay Iyay ightmay engevay myay ousin’scay eathday.Adylay Apuletcay.Eway illway avehay engeancevay orfay ityay, earfay outhay otnay.Enthay eepway onay oremay.I’llyay endsay otay oneyay inyay Antuamay, Erewhay atthay amesay anish’dbay unagateray othday ivelay, Allshay ivegay imhay uchsay anyay unaccustom’dyay amdray Atthay ehay allshay oonsay eepkay Alttybay ompanycay: Andyay enthay Iyay opehay outhay iltway ebay atisfiedsay.Ulietjay.Indeedyay Iyay evernay allshay ebay atisfiedsay Ithway Omeoray illtay Iyay eholdbay im—deadhay— Isyay myay oorpay earthay osay orfay ayay insmankay ex’dvay.Adammay, ifyay ouyay ouldcay indfay outyay utbay ayay anmay Otay earbay ayay oisonpay, Iyay ouldway empertay ityay, Atthay Omeoray ouldshay uponyay eceiptray ereofthay, Oonsay eepslay inyay uietqay.Oyay, owhay myay earthay abhorsyay Otay earhay imhay am’dnay, andyay annotcay omecay otay imhay, Otay eakwray ethay ovelay Iyay orebay myay ousincay Uponyay ishay odybay atthay athhay aughter’dslay imhay.Adylay Apuletcay.Indfay outhay ethay eansmay, andyay I’llyay indfay uchsay ayay anmay.Utbay ownay I’llyay elltay eethay oyfuljay idingstay, irlgay.Ulietjay.Andyay oyjay omescay ellway inyay uchsay ayay eedynay imetay.Atwhay areyay eythay, Iyay eseechbay ouryay adyshiplay?Adylay Apuletcay.Ellway, ellway, outhay asthay ayay arefulcay atherfay, ildchay; Oneyay owhay otay utpay eethay omfray thyay eavinesshay, Athhay ortedsay outyay ayay uddensay ayday ofyay oyjay, Atthay outhay expectsyay otnay, ornay Iyay ook’dlay otnay orfay.Ulietjay.Adammay, inyay appyhay imetay, atwhay ayday isyay atthay?Adylay Apuletcay.Arrymay, myay ildchay, earlyyay extnay Ursdaythay ornmay Ethay allantgay, oungyay, andyay oblenay entlemangay, Ethay Ountycay Arispay, atyay Aintsay Eter’spay Urchchay, Allshay appilyhay akemay eethay erethay ayay oyfuljay idebray.Ulietjay.Ownay byay Aintsay Eter’spay Urchchay, andyay Eterpay ootay, Ehay allshay otnay akemay emay erethay ayay oyfuljay idebray.Iyay onderway atyay isthay astehay, atthay Iyay ustmay edway Ereyay ehay atthay ouldshay ebay usbandhay omescay otay ooway.Iyay aypray ouyay elltay myay ordlay andyay atherfay, adammay, Iyay illway otnay arrymay etyay; andyay enwhay Iyay oday, Iyay earsway Ityay allshay ebay Omeoray, omwhay ouyay owknay Iyay atehay, Atherray anthay Arispay.Esethay areyay ewsnay Ursenay.Apuletcay.Enwhay ethay unsay etssay, ethay airyay othday izzledray ewday; Utbay orfay ethay unsetsay ofyay myay other’sbray onsay Ityay ainsray ownrightday.Owhay ownay?Ayay onduitcay, irlgay?Atwhay, illstay inyay earstay?Evermoreyay oweringshay?Inyay oneyay ittlelay odybay Outhay ounterfeitscay ayay arkbay, ayay easay, ayay indway.Orfay illstay thyay eyesyay, ichwhay Iyay aymay allcay ethay easay, Oday ebbyay andyay owflay ithway earstay; ethay arkbay thyay odybay isyay, Ailingsay inyay isthay altsay oodflay, ethay indsway, thyay ighssay, Owhay agingray ithway thyay earstay andyay eythay ithway emthay, Ithoutway ayay uddensay almcay illway oversetyay Thyay empest-tossedtay odybay.Owhay ownay, ifeway?Avehay ouyay eliver’dday otay erhay ouryay ecreeday?Adylay Apuletcay.Ayyay, irsay; utbay eshay illway onenay, eshay ivesgay ouyay anksthay.Iyay ouldway ethay oolfay ereway arriedmay otay erhay avegray.Apuletcay.Oftsay.Aketay emay ithway ouyay, aketay emay avehay oughtwray Osay orthyway ayay entlemangay otay ebay erhay idegroombray?Ulietjay.Otnay oudpray ouyay avehay, utbay ankfulthay atthay ouyay avehay.Oudpray ancay Iyay evernay ebay ofyay atwhay Iyay extnay Otay ogay ithway Arispay otay Aintsay Eter’spay Urchchay, Oryay Iyay illway agdray eethay onyay ayay urdlehay itherthay.Outyay, ouyay een-sicknessgray arrioncay!Outyay, ouyay aggagebay!Ouyay ordway.Apuletcay.Anghay eethay oungyay aggagebay, isobedientday etchwray!Iyay elltay eethay at,—getwhay eethay otay urchchay ayay Ursdaythay, Oryay evernay afteryay ooklay emay inyay ethay acefay.Eakspay otnay, eplyray otnay, oday otnay answeryay emay.Myay ingersfay itchyay.Ifeway, eway arcescay oughtthay usyay estblay Atthay Odgay adhay entlay usyay utbay isthay onlyyay ildchay; Utbay ownay Iyay eesay isthay oneyay isyay oneyay ootay uchmay, Andyay atthay eway avehay ayay ursecay inyay avinghay erhay.Outyay onyay erhay, ildinghay.Ursenay.Odgay inyay eavenhay essblay erhay.Ouyay erehay eway eednay ityay otnay.Adylay Apuletcay.Ouyay areyay ootay othay.Apuletcay.Od’sgay eadbray, ityay akesmay emay admay!Ayday, ightnay, ourhay, ideray, imetay, orkway, ayplay, Aloneyay, inyay ompanycay, illstay myay arecay athhay eenbay Otay avehay erhay atch’dmay, andyay avinghay ownay ovidedpray Ayay entlemangay ofyay oblenay arentagepay, Ofyay airfay emesnesday, outhfulyay, andyay oblynay alliedyay, Uff’dstay, asyay eythay aysay, ithway onourablehay artspay, Oportion’dpray asyay one’syay oughtthay ouldway ishway ayay anmay, Andyay enthay otay avehay ayay etchedwray ulingpay oolfay, Ayay iningwhay ammetmay, inyay erhay ortune’sfay endertay, Otay answeryay, i’ll‘ay otnay edway, Iyay annotcay ovelay, Iyay amyay ootay oungyay, Iyay aypray ouyay ardonpay emay. ’ay Utbay, andyay ouyay illway otnay edway, I’llyay ardonpay ouyay.Azegray erewhay ouyay illway, ouyay allshay otnay ousehay ithway emay.Ooklay o’ttay, inkthay on’tyay, Iyay oday otnay useyay otay emay omfray eavenhay Byay eavinglay earthyay?Omfortcay emay, ounselcay emay.Alackyay, alackyay, atthay eavenhay ouldshay actisepray atagemsstray Uponyay osay oftsay ayay ubjectsay asyay elfmysay.Atwhay ay’stsay outhay?Asthay outhay otnay ayay ordway ofyay oyjay?Omesay omfortcay, Ursenay.Ursenay.Aithfay, erehay ityay isyay.Omeoray isyay anishedbay; andyay allyay ethay orldway otay othingnay Atthay ehay aresday e’ernay omecay ackbay otay allengechay ouyay.Oryay ifyay ehay oday, ityay eedsnay ustmay ebay byay ealthstay.Enthay, incesay ethay asecay osay andsstay asyay ownay ityay othday, Iyay inkthay ityay estbay ouyay arriedmay ithway ethay Ountycay.Oyay, e’shay ayay ovelylay entlemangay.Omeo’sray ayay ishcloutday otay imhay.Anyay eagleyay, adammay, Athhay otnay osay eengray, osay uickqay, osay airfay anyay eyeyay Asyay Arispay athhay.Eshrewbay myay eryvay earthay, Iyay inkthay ouyay areyay appyhay inyay isthay econdsay atchmay, Orfay ityay excelsyay ouryay irstfay: oryay ifyay ityay idday otnay, Ouryay irstfay isyay eadday, oryay ere’tway asyay oodgay ehay ereway, Asyay ivinglay erehay andyay ouyay onay useyay ofyay imhay.Ulietjay.Eakestspay outhay omfray thyay andyay elltay myay adylay Iyay amyay onegay, Avinghay ispleas’dday myay atherfay, otay Awrencelay’ ellcay, Otay akemay onfessioncay andyay otay ebay absolv’dyay.Ursenay.Arrymay, Iyay illway; andyay isthay isyay iselyway oneday.exit[_ay. _]ay Ulietjay.Ancientyay amnationday!Oyay ostmay ickedway iendfay!Isyay ityay oremay insay otay ishway emay usthay orswornfay, Oryay otay ispraiseday myay ordlay ithway atthay amesay onguetay Ichwhay eshay athhay ais’dpray imhay ithway aboveyay omparecay Osay anymay ousandthay imestay?Ogay, ounsellorcay.Outhay andyay myay osombay enceforthhay allshay ebay
