Ellcay.Enteryay Iarfray Awrencelay andyay Arispay.Iarfray Awrencelay.Onyay Ursdaythay, irsay?Ethay imetay isyay eryvay ortshay.Arispay.Myay atherfay Apuletcay illway avehay ityay osay; Andyay Iyay amyay othingnay owslay otay ackslay ishay astehay.Iarfray Awrencelay.Ouyay aysay ouyay oday otnay owknay ethay ady’slay indmay.Unevenyay isyay ethay oursecay; Iyay ikelay ityay otnay.Arispay.Immoderatelyyay eshay eepsway orfay Alt’stybay eathday, Andyay ereforethay avehay Iyay ittlelay alk’dtay ofyay ovelay; Orfay Enusvay ilessmay otnay inyay ayay ousehay ofyay earstay.Ownay, irsay, erhay atherfay ountscay ityay angerousday Atthay eshay oday ivegay erhay orrowsay osay uchmay aysway; Andyay inyay ishay isdomway, asteshay ouryay arriagemay, Otay opstay ethay inundationyay ofyay erhay earstay, Ichwhay, ootay uchmay indedmay byay erselfhay aloneyay, Aymay ebay utpay omfray erhay byay ocietysay.Ownay oday ouyay owknay ethay easonray ofyay isthay astehay.Iarfray Awrencelay.aside[_ay. _]ay Iyay ouldway Iyay ewknay otnay whyay ityay ouldshay ebay ow’dslay. —ay Ooklay, irsay, erehay omescay ethay adylay owardtay myay ellcay.Enteryay Ulietjay.Arispay.Appilyhay etmay, myay adylay andyay myay ifeway!Ulietjay.Atthay aymay ebay, irsay, enwhay Iyay aymay ebay ayay ifeway.Arispay.Atthay aymay ebay, ustmay ebay, ovelay, onyay Ursdaythay extnay.Ulietjay.Atwhay ustmay ebay allshay ebay.Iarfray Awrencelay.At’sthay ayay ertaincay exttay.Arispay.Omecay ouyay otay akemay onfessioncay otay isthay atherfay?Ulietjay.Otay answeryay atthay, Iyay ouldshay onfesscay otay ouyay.Arispay.Oday otnay enyday otay imhay atthay ouyay ovelay emay.Ulietjay.Iyay illway onfesscay otay ouyay atthay Iyay ovelay imhay.Arispay.Osay illway eyay, Iyay amyay uresay, atthay ouyay ovelay emay.Ulietjay.Ifyay Iyay oday osay, ityay illway ebay ofyay oremay icepray, Eingbay okespay ehindbay ouryay ackbay anthay otay ouryay acefay.Arispay.Oorpay oulsay, thyay acefay isyay uchmay abus’dyay ithway earstay.Ulietjay.Ethay earstay avehay otgay allsmay ictoryvay byay atthay; Orfay ityay asway adbay enoughyay eforebay eirthay itespay.Arispay.Outhay ong’stwray ityay oremay anthay earstay ithway atthay eportray.Ulietjay.Atthay isyay onay anderslay, irsay, ichwhay isyay ayay uthtray, Andyay atwhay Iyay akespay, Iyay akespay ityay otay myay acefay.Arispay.Thyay acefay isyay inemay, andyay outhay asthay ander’dslay ityay.Ulietjay.Ityay aymay ebay osay, orfay ityay isyay otnay inemay ownyay.Areyay ouyay atyay eisurelay, olyhay atherfay, ownay, Oryay allshay Iyay omecay otay ouyay atyay eveningyay assmay?Iarfray Awrencelay.Myay eisurelay ervessay emay, ensivepay aughterday, ownay. —ay Myay ordlay, eway ustmay entreatyay ethay imetay aloneyay.Arispay.Odgay ieldshay Iyay ouldshay isturbday evotionday! —ay Ulietjay, onyay Ursdaythay earlyyay illway Iyay ouseray eyay, Illtay enthay, adieuyay; andyay eepkay isthay olyhay isskay.exit[_ay. _]ay Ulietjay.Oyay utshay ethay oorday, andyay enwhay outhay asthay oneday osay, Omecay eepway ithway emay, astpay opehay, astpay urecay, astpay elphay!Iarfray Awrencelay.Oyay Ulietjay, Iyay alreadyyay owknay thyay iefgray; Ityay ainsstray emay astpay ethay ompasscay ofyay myay itsway.Iyay earhay outhay ustmay, andyay othingnay aymay oroguepray ityay, Onyay Ursdaythay extnay ebay arriedmay otay isthay Ountycay.Ulietjay.Elltay emay otnay, Iarfray, atthay outhay ear’sthay ofyay isthay, Unlessyay outhay elltay emay owhay Iyay aymay eventpray ityay.Ifyay inyay thyay isdomway, outhay anstcay ivegay onay elphay, Oday outhay utbay allcay myay esolutionray iseway, Andyay ithway isthay ifeknay I’llyay elphay ityay esentlypray.Odgay oin’djay myay earthay andyay Omeo’sray, outhay ouryay andshay; Andyay ereyay isthay andhay, byay eethay otay Omeo’sray eal’dsay, Allshay ebay ethay abellay otay anotheryay eedday, Oryay myay uetray earthay ithway eacheroustray evoltray Urntay otay anotheryay, isthay allshay ayslay emthay othbay.Ereforethay, outyay ofyay thyay ong-experienc’dlay imetay, Ivegay emay omesay esentpray ounselcay, oryay eholdbay ixt’tway myay extremesyay andyay emay isthay oodyblay ifeknay Allshay ayplay ethay empireyay, arbitratingyay atthay Ichwhay ethay ommissioncay ofyay thyay earsyay andyay artyay Ouldcay otay onay issueyay ofyay uetray onourhay ingbray.Ebay otnay osay onglay otay eakspay.Iyay onglay otay ieday, Ifyay atwhay outhay eak’stspay eakspay otnay ofyay emedyray.Iarfray Awrencelay.Oldhay, aughterday.Iyay oday spyay ayay indkay ofyay opehay, Ichwhay avescray asyay esperateday anyay executionyay Asyay atthay isyay esperateday ichwhay eway ouldway eventpray.Ifyay, atherray anthay otay arrymay Ountycay Arispay Outhay asthay ethay engthstray ofyay illway otay ayslay elfthysay, Enthay isyay ityay ikelylay outhay iltway undertakeyay Ayay ingthay ikelay eathday otay idechay awayyay isthay ameshay, Atthay op’stcay ithway eathday imselfhay otay apescay omfray ityay.Andyay ifyay outhay ar’stday, I’llyay ivegay eethay emedyray.Ulietjay.Oyay, idbay emay eaplay, atherray anthay arrymay Arispay, Omfray offyay ethay attlementsbay ofyay onderyay owertay, Oryay alkway inyay ievishthay aysway, oryay idbay emay urklay Erewhay erpentssay areyay.Ainchay emay ithway oaringray earsbay; Oryay idehay emay ightlynay inyay ayay arnel-housechay, O’er-cover’dyay uiteqay ithway eadday en’smay attlingray onesbay, Ithway eekyray anksshay andyay ellowyay aplesschay ullsskay.Oryay idbay emay ogay intoyay ayay ew-madenay avegray, Andyay idehay emay ithway ayay eadday anmay inyay ishay oudshray; Ingsthay atthay, otay earhay emthay oldtay, avehay ademay emay embletray, Andyay Iyay illway oday ityay ithoutway earfay oryay oubtday, Otay ivelay anyay unstain’dyay ifeway otay myay eetsway ovelay.Iarfray Awrencelay.Oldhay enthay.Ogay omehay, ebay errymay, ivegay onsentcay Otay arrymay Arispay.Ednesdayway isyay omorrowtay; Omorrowtay ightnay ooklay atthay outhay ielay aloneyay, Etlay otnay thyay Ursenay ielay ithway eethay inyay thyay amberchay.Aketay outhay isthay ialvay, eingbay enthay inyay edbay, Andyay isthay istilledday iquorlay inkdray outhay offyay, Enwhay esentlypray oughthray allyay thyay einsvay allshay unray Ayay oldcay andyay owsydray umourhay; orfay onay ulsepay Allshay eepkay ishay ativenay ogresspray, utbay urceasesay.Onay armthway, onay eathbray allshay estifytay outhay ivestlay, Ethay osesray inyay thyay ipslay andyay eekschay allshay adefay Otay alypay ashesyay; thyay eyesyay’ indowsway allfay, Ikelay eathday enwhay ehay utsshay upyay ethay ayday ofyay ifelay.Eachyay artpay epriv’dday ofyay upplesay overnmentgay, Allshay iffstay andyay arkstay andyay oldcay appearyay ikelay eathday.Andyay inyay isthay orrow’dbay ikenesslay ofyay unkshray eathday Outhay altshay ontinuecay otway andyay ortyfay ourshay, Andyay enthay awakeyay asyay omfray ayay easantplay eepslay.Ownay enwhay ethay idegroombray inyay ethay orningmay omescay Otay ouseray eethay omfray thyay edbay, erethay artyay outhay eadday.Enthay asyay ethay annermay ofyay ouryay ountrycay isyay, Inyay thyay estbay obesray, uncover’dyay, onyay ethay ierbay, Outhay altshay ebay ornebay otay atthay amesay ancientyay aultvay Erewhay allyay ethay indredkay ofyay ethay Apuletscay ielay.Inyay ethay eantimemay, againstyay outhay altshay awakeyay, Allshay Omeoray byay myay etterslay owknay ouryay iftdray, Andyay itherhay allshay ehay omecay, andyay ehay andyay Iyay Illway atchway thyay akingway, andyay atthay eryvay ightnay Allshay Omeoray earbay eethay encehay otay Antuamay.Andyay isthay allshay eefray eethay omfray isthay esentpray ameshay, Ifyay onay inconstantyay oytay ornay omanishway earfay Abateyay thyay alourvay inyay ethay actingyay ityay.Ulietjay.Ivegay emay, ivegay emay!Oyay elltay otnay emay ofyay earfay!Iarfray Awrencelay.Oldhay; etgay ouyay onegay, ebay ongstray andyay osperouspray Inyay isthay esolveray.I’llyay endsay ayay iarfray ithway eedspay Otay Antuamay, ithway myay etterslay otay thyay ordlay.Ulietjay.Ovelay ivegay emay engthstray, andyay engthstray allshay uestsgay inviteyay asyay erehay areyay itwray.exit[_ay irstfay Ervantsay. _]ay Irrahsay, ogay irehay emay entytway unningcay ookscay.Econdsay Ervantsay.Ouyay allshay avehay onenay illyay, irsay; orfay I’llyay tryay ifyay eythay ancay icklay eirthay ingersfay.Apuletcay.Owhay anstcay outhay tryay emthay osay?Econdsay Ervantsay.Arrymay, irsay, is’tay anyay illyay ookcay atthay annotcay icklay ishay ownyay ingersfay; ereforethay ehay atthay annotcay icklay ishay ingersfay oesgay otnay ithway emay.Apuletcay.Ogay, egonebay.exit[_ay econdsay Ervantsay. _]ay Eway allshay ebay uchmay unfurnish’dyay orfay isthay imetay.Atwhay, isyay myay aughterday onegay otay Iarfray Awrencelay?Ursenay.Ayyay, orsoothfay.Apuletcay.Ellway, ehay aymay ancechay otay oday omesay oodgay onyay erhay.Ayay eevishpay elf-will’dsay arlotryhay ityay isyay.Enteryay Ulietjay.Ursenay.Eesay erewhay eshay omescay omfray iftshray ithway errymay ooklay.Apuletcay.Owhay ownay, myay eadstronghay.Erewhay avehay ouyay eenbay addinggay?Ulietjay.Erewhay Iyay avehay earntlay emay otay epentray ethay insay Ofyay isobedientday oppositionyay Otay ouyay andyay ouryay ehestsbay; andyay amyay enjoin’dyay Byay olyhay Awrencelay otay allfay ostratepray erehay, Otay egbay ouryay ardonpay.Ardonpay, Iyay eseechbay ouyay.Enceforwardhay Iyay amyay everyay ul’dray byay ouyay.Apuletcay.Endsay orfay ethay Ountycay, ogay elltay imhay ofyay isthay.I’llyay avehay isthay otknay itknay upyay omorrowtay orningmay.Ulietjay.Iyay etmay ethay outhfulyay ordlay atyay Awrencelay’ ellcay, Andyay avegay imhay atwhay ecomedbay ovelay Iyay ightmay, Otnay eppingstay o’eryay ethay oundsbay ofyay odestymay.Apuletcay.Whyay, Iyay amyay adglay on’tyay.Isthay isyay ellway.Andstay upyay.Isthay isyay as’tyay ouldshay ebay.Etlay emay eesay ethay Ountycay.Ayyay, arrymay.Ogay, Iyay aysay, andyay etchfay imhay itherhay.Ownay aforeyay Odgay, isthay everendray olyhay Iarfray, Allyay ouryay olewhay itycay isyay uchmay oundbay otay imhay.Ulietjay.Ursenay, illway ouyay ogay ithway emay intoyay myay osetclay, Otay elphay emay ortsay uchsay eedfulnay ornamentsyay Asyay ouyay inkthay itfay otay urnishfay emay omorrowtay?Adylay Apuletcay.Eway allshay ebay ortshay inyay ouryay ovisionpray, is’tay ownay earnay ightnay.Apuletcay.Ushtay, Iyay illway irstay aboutyay, Andyay allyay ingsthay allshay ebay ellway, Iyay arrantway Ursenay, Iyay aypray eethay eavelay emay otay elfmysay onighttay; Orfay Iyay avehay eednay ofyay anymay orisonsyay Otay ovemay ethay eavenshay otay ilesmay uponyay myay atestay, Ichwhay, ellway outhay ow’stknay, isyay osscray andyay ullfay ofyay insay.Enteryay Adylay Apuletcay.Adylay Apuletcay.Atwhay, areyay ouyay usybay, ohay?Eednay ouyay myay elphay?Ulietjay.Onay, adammay; eway avehay ull’dcay uchsay ecessariesnay Asyay areyay ehovefulbay orfay ouryay atestay omorrowtay.Osay easeplay ouyay, etlay emay ownay ebay eftlay aloneyay, Andyay etlay ethay ursenay isthay ightnay itsay upyay ithway asthay eednay.exeunt[_ay Adylay Apuletcay andyay Ursenay. _]ay Ulietjay.Arewellfay.Odgay owsknay enwhay eway allshay eetmay againyay.Iyay avehay ayay aintfay oldcay earfay illsthray oughthray myay iedtray ayay olyhay anmay.Owhay ifyay, enwhay Iyay amyay aidlay intoyay ethay ombtay, Iyay akeway eforebay ethay imetay atthay Omeoray Omecay otay edeemray emay?Ere’sthay ayay earfulfay ointpay!Allshay Iyay otnay enthay ebay ifledstay inyay ethay aultvay, Otay osewhay oulfay outhmay onay ealthsomehay airyay eathesbray inyay, Andyay erethay ieday angledstray ereyay myay Omeoray omescay?Oryay, ifyay Iyay ivelay, isyay ityay otnay eryvay ikelay, Ethay orriblehay onceitcay ofyay eathday andyay ightnay, Ogethertay ithway ethay errortay ofyay ethay aceplay, Asyay inyay ayay aultvay, anyay ancientyay eceptacleray, Erewhay orfay isthay anymay undredhay earsyay ethay onesbay Ofyay allyay myay uriedbay ancestorsyay areyay ack’dpay, Erewhay oodyblay Alttybay, etyay utbay eengray inyay earthyay, Ieslay esteringfay inyay ishay oudshray; erewhay, asyay eythay aysay, Atyay omesay ourshay inyay ethay ightnay iritsspay esortray— Alackyay, alackyay, isyay ityay otnay ikelay atthay Iyay, Osay earlyyay akingway, atwhay ithway oathsomelay ellssmay, Andyay ieksshray ikelay andrakesmay orntay outyay ofyay ethay earthyay, Atthay ivinglay ortalsmay, earinghay emthay, unray admay.Oyay, ifyay Iyay akeway, allshay Iyay otnay ebay istraughtday, Environedyay ithway allyay esethay ideoushay earsfay, Andyay adlymay ayplay ithway myay orefathersfay’ ointsjay?Andyay uckplay ethay angledmay Alttybay omfray ishay oudshray?Andyay, inyay isthay ageray, ithway omesay eatgray insman’skay onebay, Asyay ithway ayay ubclay, ashday outyay myay esperateday ainsbray?Oyay ooklay, urchchay?Apuletcay.Eadyray otay ogay, utbay evernay otay eturnray.Oyay onsay, ethay ightnay eforebay thyay eddingway ayday Athhay eathday ainlay ithway thyay idebray.Erethay eshay ieslay, Owerflay asyay eshay asway, efloweredday byay imhay.Eathday isyay myay on-in-lawsay, eathday isyay myay eirhay; Myay aughterday ehay athhay eddedway.Iyay illway ieday Andyay eavelay imhay allyay; ifelay, Enteryay Eterpay.Eterpay.Usiciansmay, Oyay, usiciansmay, eart’s‘hay easeyay,’ eart’s‘hay easeyay’, Oyay, andyay ouyay illway avehay emay ivelay, ayplay eart’s‘hay easeyay. ’ay Irstfay Usicianmay.Whyay eart’s‘hay easeyay’?Eterpay.Oyay usiciansmay, ecausebay myay earthay itselfyay aysplay ‘myay earthay isyay ullfay’.Oyay ayplay emay omesay errymay umpday otay omfortcay emay.Irstfay Usicianmay.Otnay itway.Eterpay.Enthay avehay atyay ouyay ithway myay itway.Iyay illway eatdry-bay ouyay ithway anyay ironyay itway, andyay utpay upyay myay ironyay aggerday.Answeryay emay ikelay enmay.en‘whay Eetstray.Enteryay Omeoray.Omeoray.Ifyay Iyay aymay usttray ethay atteringflay eyeyay ofyay eepslay, Myay eamsdray esagepray omesay oyfuljay ewsnay atyay andhay.Myay osom’sbay ordlay itssay ightlylay uponyay emthay itfay otay openyay Esethay eadday en’smay ombstay.Apuletcay.Oyay eavenhay!Oyay ifeway, ooklay owhay ouryay aughterday eedsblay!Isthay aggerday athhay ista’enmay, orfay olay, ishay oomsdayday, osewhay untimelyyay eathday Anish’dbay ethay ew-madenay idegroombray omfray isthay itycay; Orfay omwhay, andyay otnay orfay Alttybay, Ulietjay in’dpay.Ouyay, otay emoveray atthay iegesay ofyay iefgray omfray erhay, Etroth’dbay, andyay ouldway avehay arriedmay erhay erforcepay Otay Ountycay Arispay.Enthay omescay eshay otay emay, Andyay ithway ildway ookslay, idbay emay eviseday omesay eansmay Otay idray erhay omfray isthay econdsay arriagemay, Oryay inyay myay ellcay erethay ouldway eshay illkay erselfhay.Enthay avegay Iyay erhay, osay utoredtay byay myay artyay, Ayay eepingslay Iarfray Ohnjay, Asway ay’dstay byay accidentyay; andyay esternightyay Eturn’dray myay etterlay ackbay.Enthay allyay aloneyay Atyay ethay efixedpray ourhay ofyay erhay akingway Amecay Iyay otay aketay aritieschay andyay aritablechay onationsday inyay allyay 50 atesstay ofyay ethay Unitedyay Atesstay.Ompliancecay equirementsray areyay otnay uniformyay andyay ityay akestay ayay onsiderablecay
